### dimension: schemas
Claude SUMMARY: The structured-output SCHEMAS themselves are well-hardened against model variance: every model in src/polaris_graph/schemas.py uses plain str/float fields with default=, enum-like values (verdict, decision, convergence_assessment, gap_severity, analytical_focus) are plain str NOT Literal/enum, and lenient @model_validator(mode='before') normalizers map alt-field-names and coerce types AFTER parsing. The 4-role judges, sentinel, mirror adapters, entailment_judge, semantic_conflict_detector and evidence_distiller all use loose response_format={'type':'json_object'} (the SAFE mode). The single real schema-side chokepoint is the strict json_schema path in OpenRouterClient.generate_structured (openrouter_client.py:3108-3121): it hardcodes strict:True and the pydantic model_json_schema() it emits is structurally incompatible with OpenAI-style provider strict mode (no additionalProperties:false because no schema sets model_config extra='forbid'; defaulted fields are NOT in required; nested $ref/$defs and anyOf-for-Optional). This is exactly the I-ready-018 404 disease ('No endpoints found' when strict json_schema collides with reasoning + provider.require_parameters). The current guard is a HARDCODED model allowlist (_REASONING_FIRST_MODELS at line 3110) that only protects deepseek-v4-pro/-flash and glm-5.x; any other locked-or-future slug run with reasoning OFF (an agent client pointed at qwen3.6 or minimax-m2, or any new model the operator configures) still attaches strict:True an

If the first failure was a strict-schema provider rejection (404/400), the retry repeats the same wire shape and fails the same way, burning a second full reasoning-token round before any recovery.
  CURRENT: messages[-1] = retry_prompt; result = await self._call(..., response_format=response_format, ...)  # same strict response_format reused
  CLAUDE_FIX: On the validation/JSON-decode retry, set response_format=None (or {'type':'json_object'}) for the retry _call so a strict-induced provider rejection cannot recur; rely on json_hint + _extract_json_from_text + _repair_truncated_json recovery already present. Optionally gate the downgrade behind PG_ST
  WHY: A strict-schema 400/404 is deterministic, not transient: retrying with the same response_format cannot succeed. On the locked reasoning-first generator a retry can cost minutes of reasoning tokens (the operator's exact pain point: a 3-hour run dying late). The retry should DROP strict (downgrade to json_object or None) so the second attempt can actually parse via the prompt-based path.

- [P3] src/polaris_graph/schemas.py:705-707 (ThemeResult.helpfulness)
  WHAT: helpfulness is the ONLY field in the whole schema module carrying hard numeric constraints (ge=0, le=100). Under provider strict json_schema these become minimum/maximum keywords some providers reject under strict, and on the pydantic side a model returning 0-1 or 0-1000 scaled scores fails validation and that theme is dropped.
  CURRENT: helpfulness: int = Field(default=50, ge=0, le=100)
  CLAUDE_FIX: Drop ge/le and add a coerce-and-clamp @field_validator(mode='before') mirroring AtomicFact.clamp_scores (parse str/float, scale, clamp into 0-100) so out-of-range or mis-scaled values are corrected, not dropped. This also removes the lone hard-bound that aggravates provider strict mode.
  WHY: BatchClusterResult/ThemeResult is on the live map-reduce clustering path (synthesizer.py:4820). If a model emits helpfulness as 0.7, 95.0-as-fraction, or 250, the ge/le bound raises ValidationError and the theme is dropped by the batch filter, thinning clusters. Under strict provider mode the min/max keywords can also contribute to schema-invalid rejections. Inconsistent with every other score fie

- [P3] src/polaris_graph/llm/openrouter_client.py:3060 (function default; call sites e.g. agents/analyzer.py:2063 override to 16384)
  WHAT: generate_structured default max_tokens=8192 is a hardcoded function-default; not every caller overrides it with an env-driven value. A schema-heavy batch (SourceAnalysisBatch with up to 15 facts x N sources, ReportOutline with many sections) can exceed 8192 output tokens, truncating the JSON.
  CURRENT: max_tokens: int = 8192 (function default literal)
  CLAUDE_FIX: Default max_tokens from an env var: max_tokens: int = int(os.getenv('PG_STRUCTURED_MAX_TOKENS','16384')) (raise the default to a generous, usage-billed cap per the MAX-tokens directive) so structured batches are not truncated, while individual callers may still pass tighter per-call budgets.
  WHY: Same family as the token-starvation disease (I-arch-003): an 8192 cap truncates a large structured batch, dropping facts/sections after JSON-repair salvage, which thins evidence/breadth. It is a hardcoded magic number rather than an env-governed budget, so an operator cannot raise the structured-output ceiling globally without editing code.

# POLARIS PROJECT - Operational Directives

CRITICAL: This file (CLAUDE.md) MUST be read in its entirety at the start of EVERY session and immediately following ANY restart. Failure to adhere to these directives constitutes a critical operational failure. See §3 for the mandatory startup protocol.

Document Class: Operational, Binding, Project-Specific
Scope: All POLARIS development, research pipeline implementation, and maintenance tasks.

## §-1. STANDING EVALUATION & DEBUG STANDARDS (binding for ALL work)

**These three standards override every other directive in this file when they conflict. §-1.1 and §-1.2 were flagged by user 2026-05-09 night as repeat-violation patterns; §-1.3 was operator-locked 2026-06-13 after a full day lost to symptom-patching.**

### §-1.1 Line-by-line audit standard (clinical-safety-critical)

Every evaluation, audit, comparison, benchmark, regression check, BEAT-BOTH framing, or quality assessment **MUST** be:

1. **Claim-by-claim** against the actually-fetched source content (cited span text, not title or abstract).
2. **Reasoning-step-by-reasoning-step** — verify each piece of reasoning follows from the cited evidence.
3. **Citation-by-citation** — verify each citation is appropriate for the claim.
4. **Apply industrial benchmarks** appropriate to the domain:
   - Clinical: PRISMA 2020, AMSTAR-2, GRADE per claim, ICMJE authorship/COI, ICH-GCP for trial methods, Cochrane RoB 2 / ROBINS-I / QUADAS-2.
   - Regulatory: jurisdiction-specific (FDA label, EMA SmPC, Health Canada PM, NICE TA, MHRA AR, TGA PI, PMDA review, NMPA labeling).
   - Methodology: appropriate risk-of-bias tool for the study type.
5. **Both Claude and Codex run independent line-by-line audits in parallel.** Cross-review combines findings.
6. Per-claim verdict: **VERIFIED / PARTIAL / UNSUPPORTED / FABRICATED / UNREACHABLE** with the specific cited span quote that supports the verdict.

**STRICTLY BANNED:**
- Word counts / citation counts / unique-source counts as quality signals
- Pattern presence ("does the report mention 'tirzepatide'?")
- Sample-based audits ("we audited 5 of 50 claims")
- String-presence PASS/FAIL checks (e.g., gate tables)
- Metadata comparison (e.g., "ChatGPT has 27 contradictions, POLARIS has 3, so ChatGPT is better" — this framing is **lethal in clinical context**)

**Why this matters:** clinical context. Pattern-matching evaluation will miss real fabrications. Patients can be hurt by a wrong dose, wrong contraindication, wrong indication population that survived a metadata check. "It is lethal" is literal.

**Application:** when the user asks for an audit/evaluation/comparison/benchmark, line-by-line is the ONLY acceptable answer. If you propose a metadata or pattern audit, you have failed the user.

### §-1.2 Standard debug workflow (no §3.0 bypass)

Every task / bug / issue follows this exact sequence — no shortcuts:

1. **GitHub Issue FIRST.** `gh issue create` BEFORE any branch, any code, any brief. Title format: `I-<prefix>-NNN — <summary>`. Body has acceptance criteria. **No exceptions.**
2. **Comprehensive grep/scan adjacent files.** Before writing the brief, grep all call sites, consumers, downstream rule checks, and tests touching the area. List them in the brief under **"Files I have ALSO checked and they're clean: [...]"**.
3. **Smoke test offline.** Unit tests run; if the change touches the pipeline, run a minimal smoke test (single sentence, single section) BEFORE launching a full sweep. Full sweeps are NOT smoke tests.
4. **Brief Codex.** Open with the iter-1 cap directive (§8.3.1 verbatim). Include the adjacent-file scan results so Codex VERIFIES rather than discovers.
5. **Goal: 1-2 iters per task, not 5.** The 5-cap is a backstop, not a target.
6. **If a big bug surfaces and cannot be resolved in 5 iters, mark it as URGENT new GitHub Issue and resolve it FIRST.** Do not let cap-5 force-approve a real production blocker.
7. **Close the GitHub Issue when the PR merges.** Do not leave resolved issues open.

**Ordering vs §3.1 boot ritual + §3.0 halt gates:** §-1.2 governs *task-work* tool calls. The §3.1 step-0 canonical-pin verification, CHARTER+PLAN SHA pins (§10), halt-marker check (`state/halt_*`), and any active halt gate ALWAYS run first. Only after those pass does the issue-driven sequence below kick in.

**Application:** for the assigned task, the FIRST *task-work* tool call (after boot ritual + halt checks) is `gh issue create` or `gh issue view`. The SECOND is comprehensive grep. The THIRD is offline smoke test. THEN brief Codex. Anything else is a §3.0 violation.

### §-1.3 Deep-research pipeline architecture DNA (operator-locked 2026-06-13)

**The pipeline is WEIGHT-AND-CONSOLIDATE, not FILTER-AND-CAP.** Locked by the operator after a full day was lost to symptom-patching the pipeline with hardcoded caps/targets/thinners to hit a breadth NUMBER. Three binding principles govern every retrieval/selection/composition design decision:

1. **WEIGHT, DON'T FILTER.** Every relevant source flows through to composition carrying a credibility **weight** (peer-review status, journal/venue reputation, gov / institute / news / social media). Do NOT hard-drop a source to hit a number. Social media STAYS at low weight — sometimes it reports a real journal. The tier classifier (T1–T7) and `authority_score` ARE the weighting system: use them as a per-citation **weight surfaced to the user**, never as a rank-then-drop hard filter.

2. **CONSOLIDATE, DON'T DROP.** Group sources that carry the SAME claim into a **basket**. Repetition is **corroboration** — the entire point of consolidate / distill / map-reduce. Multiple citations per claim is GOOD and expected. `finding_dedup` / `fact_dedup` must CONSOLIDATE (keep ALL sources per claim as multi-citation) and operate on **qualitative** claims too — never delete corroborating sources, never restrict to numeric-only.

3. **BASKET FAITHFULNESS.** Decide a claim's faithfulness against its **whole basket** of supporting sources, never a single URL/span — single-source verification is a blind spot. The verdict carries the corroboration (count + weights + agreement). This **STRENGTHENS** faithfulness; it NEVER relaxes it.

**THE ONLY HARD GATE is the faithfulness engine** (strict_verify / NLI entailment / 4-role D8 / provenance / span-grounding). Everything else is a WEIGHT or a CONSOLIDATION — never a DROP / CAP / THIN / TARGET.

**BANNED anti-pattern (the day-waster):** bolting hardcoded caps / targets / thinners / hard-filters onto the pipeline to make a breadth number go up (`PG_SPAN_PER_SOURCE_CITE_CAP`, `PG_LEGACY_SECTION_BREADTH_TARGET`, `PG_BREADTH_CANARY_MIN`, scope hard-filter, and similar). They FIGHT the architecture. Breadth and quality **EMERGE** from honest weighted multi-attribution; they are never forced. If you find yourself adding a knob to make a number hit a target — STOP. That is the bug.

**SURGICAL, NOT REWRITE.** The good machinery already exists — STORM retrieval, Zyte/crawl4ai/distill, the tier classifier (= weighting), `finding_dedup`/`fact_dedup` (= consolidation), the faithfulness engine. RE-WIRE it to the right semantics (weight not filter; consolidate-keep-all not drop; basket not single-span) and DELETE only the specific number-forcing bolt-ons. Do not over-kill.

Canonical detail lives in `docs/polaris_pipeline_canonical.md` and the forensic design doc `docs/pipeline_architecture_forensic_2026_06_13.md`. GitHub anchor: **I-arch-001 (#1245)**.

## §0. Core Identity and Operational Mode

**0.1 Identity:** You operate as a Senior Software Engineer/AI Agent building POLARIS - a production-grade research pipeline. Your responsibility is the high-fidelity implementation of reproducible, fully documented, and production-ready systems.

**0.2 Primary Directive:** Implement the Active Project Definition (APD) as defined in §1.1.
- **Rigor:** Execute without omission, ad-hoc simplification, or corner-cutting. Do not be sloppy. Do not simplify. Do not silently degrade functionality or quality.
- **Exploration:** During exploratory phases where the APD is intentionally broad, the directive is to clarify intent, deliver high-value iterations, and rigorously document findings and the evolution of the scope (LAW I).

**0.3 Operational Mode (Mandatory Extended Thinking):** You must always engage extended thinking capabilities for planning. Every task requires this rigorous process:
1. **Analyze:** Deconstruct the request and synthesize the current APD (§1.1).
2. **Research:** Proactively search online for the latest best practices, libraries, and solutions (LAW III).
3. **Plan:** Formulate a detailed, step-by-step execution plan, considering edge cases and alternatives.
4. **Execute:** Implement the plan rigorously, ensuring synchronization (LAW I).
5. **Verify:** Validate the output against requirements and log the evidence (LAW II).
6. **Record:** Update all mandatory documentation and state files (§2).

The reasoning derived from steps 1-3 MUST be captured in the RATIONALE section of the session log (§2.2).

## §1. The LAWS (Non-Negotiable Directives)

These LAWS supersede all other instructions.

### LAW I — Active Definition and Synchronization
You must adhere strictly to the Active Project Definition (APD) and ensure its components are coherent.

**1.1 Active Project Definition (APD) Hierarchy** (updated 2026-05-05 per polaris-restart Plan §9.1 issue-driven workflow): The APD is the dynamic source of truth for the project's current goals. It is derived, in order of precedence, from:
1. Current Session Instructions: Explicit requests and clarifications made during the active session.
2. `state/active_issue.json` (The Active Work): currently in_progress GitHub Issue per `state/polaris_restart/issue_breakdown.md`. Cannot start Issue N+1 until Issue N completed.
3. `state/polaris_restart/issue_breakdown.md` (The Scope): 134 issues, Codex APPROVE iter 4 on 2026-05-05. Per-Issue GREEN criteria. Authoritative for what's "done" in issue-driven workflow.
4. `state/polaris_restart/plan.md` (The Restart Plan): Codex APPROVE iter 4. Defines role split, halt conditions, mechanical gates.
5. `docs/carney_delivery_plan_v6_2.md` (The Long-term Mission): canonical 18-week plan, hash-pinned via `docs/canonical_pin.txt`. Re-read at every session-resume.
6. Recent `logs/session_log.md` (The History).
7. `architecture.md` (The Baseline).
8. `docs/task_acceptance_matrix.yaml` (HISTORICAL — Plan-v13-era pre-Issue tracking; matrix-decommission scheduled as post-Cleanup-PR-8 follow-up PR).

**1.2 Mandatory Synchronization:** If a higher-priority item contradicts a lower-priority item, the lower-priority documentation MUST be updated immediately to reflect the higher-priority truth. This synchronization must occur before execution proceeds and must be logged (§2.2).

**1.3 Adherence:** No requirement derived from the synchronized APD may be altered, simplified, or omitted without following the protocols in §6.

### LAW II — No Fake Working (Evidence Required)
- **Forbidden:** Placeholders, mocked data (outside tests/fixtures/), silent downgrades, "demo-only" hacks.
- **Evidence:** Claims of completion require verifiable proof logged in the session log: created files, sizes/counts, checksums, and successful test outputs or key findings.
- **Data & Execution Integrity:**
  - Real Data Only: Use ONLY real data from verified sources. NO synthetic data, NO np.random/faker outside tests/fixtures/.
  - Fail Loudly: If data is unavailable, FAIL LOUDLY; never return empty/default values silently.
  - No Silent Fallbacks: Never silently downgrade capabilities, disable functions, or suppress errors.
  - Stop on Blockers: If a tool/dependency is missing, STOP, report the blocker, and await resolution.
  - Definition of Fixed: Do not mark an issue "fixed" unless you have a reproducible failing test that now passes AND artifacts demonstrating the fix.

### LAW III — Proactive Information Seeking
Do not rely on stale internalized knowledge. You must proactively search the internet for the latest official documentation, best practices, and solutions for every library, API, and function used.
Log all consulted resources in `logs/session_log.md`.

### LAW IV — Persistence of State (Never Forget)
The session must be resumable without loss of context.
Every significant action, decision, or finding must update the durable state files (§2).

### LAW V — Absolute Code and File Hygiene
Adhere strictly to the standards defined in §4 (Naming Conventions, Modularity, and Structure). The repository must remain clean and tidy at all times.

### LAW VI — Zero Hard-Coding
All parameters (endpoints, credentials, thresholds, file paths, batch sizes) must come from configuration files, CLI arguments, or environment variables.
Fixed values for testing must reside exclusively in `tests/fixtures/`.

### LAW VII — CLI Isolation (POLARIS-Specific)
Phases are standalone CLI scripts. They communicate ONLY through JSON files.
- Phase N reads ONLY from `outputs/P{N-1}/{vector_id}.json`
- Phase N writes ONLY to `outputs/P{N}/{vector_id}.json`
- Phase N NEVER imports code from other phases
- Shared utilities go in `src/utils/` or `src/schemas/`


## §3.0 Issue-driven workflow (mandatory, per polaris-restart Plan §9.1)

**Every unit of work is a GitHub Issue assigned in sequence per `state/polaris_restart/issue_breakdown.md`.** Cannot start Issue N+1 until Issue N is `completed` per TaskCreate state.

**Per-Issue mandatory artifacts** (CI will reject PR without these once PR-D installs the gate workflow; pre-PR-D, this is enforced by Codex review at PR time):
- `.codex/<issue_id>/brief.md` (Claude-authored, Codex-approved)
- `.codex/<issue_id>/codex_brief_verdict.txt` (APPROVE)
- `.codex/<issue_id>/codex_diff.patch` (Claude-written diff committed under this name; Codex reviews it — per plan §7.A LOCKED A2)
- `.codex/<issue_id>/codex_diff_audit.txt` (APPROVE on Red-Team checklist)
- `outputs/audits/<issue_id>/claude_audit.md` (Claude's architect review)
- **`.codex/<issue_id>/codex_visual_audit.txt` — 6th artifact, REQUIRED on PRs touching `web/app/**` or `web/components/**`** (added 2026-05-25 per I-ux-002; AAB pattern per `docs/ui_harness_research_2026_05_25.md`). Generated by `scripts/visual_review_gate.py` against the LOCKED `.codex/visual_audit_rubric.md`. CI gate `codex-visual-required` parses the final `verdict:` line. Non-UI PRs skip cleanly.

**Forbidden patterns:**
- `gh pr merge --admin` from Claude account/token (revoked per CHARTER §1)
- PR opened without all 5 artifacts above
- Issue jump (start `I-X-NNN+1` before `I-X-NNN` merged)
- "While we're at it" polish in same PR
- STATUS block / recap text between PR merge and next branch creation (per §8.2)

**Halt conditions (each emits `state/halt_<utc>_<reason>.md`):**
- canonical pin SHA mismatch
- CHARTER.md OR PLAN.md SHA pin mismatch (per §10 boot ritual + §3.1 step 0)
- issue jump attempt
- PR opened with missing artifact triple
- Codex unavailable >1h
- 2-cycle repeated root cause
- 200-LOC PR cap exceeded
- 3+ PRs queued for user in 24h (reviewer fatigue)

**Role split (per polaris-restart Plan §7.A LOCKED A2 + §7.B LOCKED B1):**
- **Claude:** writes code (briefs AND diffs). Author of `.codex/<issue_id>/brief.md` and `.codex/<issue_id>/codex_diff.patch` (Claude commits the diff, Codex reviews it).
- **Codex:** reviews. Two separate Codex calls per Issue: APPROVE on brief (acceptance criteria correctness) + APPROVE on diff (code correctness against brief). Codex is the only gate.
- **User:** spec owner + merge gate. Reads `git log` in the morning as the after-the-fact human-at-merge surface (B1 pure auto-merge).
- Claude has NO `gh pr merge --admin` authority. CI required check `polaris/codex-required` parses Codex's verdict file and gates merge.

### §3.0.1 The "Claude Codex Workflow" named trigger (operator, 2026-05-29)

**Invocation phrase:** when the operator says **"Claude Codex Workflow"** (or **"with Claude Codex Workflow"**) — and equivalently the keywords `exec:` / `task:` — it means: run the standing `polaris_task_cycle` loop (§3.0 above) **driven by the Anthropic Workflow function** as the engine, with **Codex as the only review gate**.

**Behavior bound to the phrase:**
1. Author a Workflow-function script that runs the loop in ordered phases: `BOOT → BRIEF → codex-gate(brief) → BUILD → SMOKE → codex-gate(diff) → CLOSE → NEXT`.
2. Spawn per-phase agents inside that workflow (build / smoke / Codex review); Codex review agents shell out to `env -u OPENAI_API_KEY codex exec` and **write** the verdict; parse the verdict from the **written file's last `verdict:` line** (§8.3.9), never an agent self-report.
3. Codex is the ONLY gate; two gates per issue (brief + diff), each 5-iter cap (§8.3.1).

**Operator is BLIND — visibility rule (BINDING):** the Workflow function runs in the background and its live progress is only in the `/workflows` panel, which a screen reader cannot read. So whenever the Claude Codex Workflow fires, Claude MUST **announce each workflow launch in one plain spoken line** as it fires AND **read the key result inline** (verdict + counts) when it completes — never make the operator open the `/workflows` panel.

**Canonical spec + recordings:** `.claude/workflows/polaris_task_cycle.md`; per-prompt enforcement + trigger detection in `.claude/hooks/polaris_task_cycle_reminder.py`; operator memory `feedback_claude_codex_workflow_named_trigger_2026_05_29.md`. Honest scope: it is a *process* run via the Workflow function, not one canned script — each task supplies its own brief/build/test content.

206:         surface |= set(full_control_surface(roots))
207:     surface |= set(_EXTRA_CONTROL_ENV)
208:     control_vars = sorted(surface)
209:     # reachability: enforce-by-default for real runs
210:     if not offline and reachability_prober is None:
211:         reachability_prober = real_retrieval_prober
212:     # 1. fallbacks OFF
213:     if os.environ.get("OPENROUTER_ALLOW_FALLBACKS", "true").strip().lower() not in ("false", "0", "no"):
214:         raise GateError("OPENROUTER_ALLOW_FALLBACKS must be false (it defaults TRUE)")
215:     # 2. provider routing — per-role resolution at preflight (I-bug-946 #932).
216:     # The env supplies a candidate list (comma-separated). Each role's actual served provider
217:     # is resolved via OpenRouter's per-model endpoints endpoint and pinned per role. The old
218:     # "singleton" check rejected multi-provider orders, but disjoint model provider sets
219:     # require a multi-entry order (e.g. fireworks for deepseek-v4-pro, novita for gemma).
220:     order = (os.environ.get("OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ORDER") or "").strip()
221:     provider_order_list = [p.strip() for p in order.split(",") if p.strip()]
222:     if not provider_order_list:
223:         raise GateError("OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ORDER must list at least one candidate provider")
224:     # 3. required retrieval capability — PRESENCE *and* REACHABILITY (Codex P1)
225:     missing = [c for c in _REQUIRED_RETRIEVAL_CREDS if not os.environ.get(c)]
226:     if missing:
227:         raise GateError(f"required retrieval credentials absent — not full-power: {missing}")
228:     if reachability_prober is not None:
229:         for cred, backend in _REQUIRED_RETRIEVAL_CREDS_TO_BACKENDS.items():
230:             if not reachability_prober(backend):
231:                 raise GateError(f"retrieval backend {backend!r} unreachable/invalid-key — not full-power")
232:     # I-meta-002 PR-9/M4: lock-sourced role -> serving_route map. Self-host roles
233:     # (serving_route: vast_self_host*) DO NOT resolve via OpenRouter; the generator
234:     # (serving_route: openrouter) and any role absent from the lock keep the OpenRouter path.
235:     serving_routes = _role_serving_routes()
236:     # 4. each role pin must declare which surrogate fields it PROVED present + a full slug
237:     for rp in role_pins:
238:         if not rp.surrogate_fields:
239:             raise GateError(f"role {rp.role}: no served-identity surrogate fields proven present")
240:         if "/" not in rp.model_slug:
241:             raise GateError(f"role {rp.role}: model_slug must be the FULL slug (provider/model), got {rp.model_slug!r}")
242:         # I-meta-002 PR-9/M4 self-host branch: a self-hosted vLLM verifier (Mirror / Sentinel /
243:         # Judge) is NOT on OpenRouter. Validate its PG_<ROLE>_BASE_URL is configured (fail-closed,
244:         # LAW VI: a self-host role with no endpoint is a deployment error, never a silent default)
245:         # and record the pinned base_url + serving_route for the post-run served==pinned check.
246:         # NO network here (env presence + lock read only — the live /v1/models identity probe is
247:         # the M2 canary, not preflight). Skip canonical_slug + OpenRouter provider resolution.
248:         route = serving_routes.get(rp.role)
249:         rp.serving_route = route
250:         if _is_self_host_route(route):
251:             base_url_env = _SELF_HOST_BASE_URL_ENV_TEMPLATE.format(role=rp.role.upper())
252:             base_url = os.environ.get(base_url_env)
253:             if not base_url:
254:                 raise GateError(
255:                     f"role {rp.role}: self-host serving_route {route!r} requires {base_url_env} "
256:                     f"to be set (the self-hosted endpoint must be configured, LAW VI)"
257:                 )
258:             rp.base_url = base_url.rstrip("/")
259:             continue
260:         # I-bug-945 (#931): resolve OpenRouter alias to its dated canonical_slug at preflight.
261:         # The catalog is the single source of truth; fail closed if the alias is unknown.
262:         # Skipped on offline runs (unit tests pass canonical_slug directly when needed).
263:         if not offline and rp.canonical_slug is None:
264:             rp.canonical_slug = resolve_canonical_slug(rp.model_slug)
265:         # I-bug-946 (#932): resolve per-role provider via /api/v1/models/<id>/endpoints.
266:         # Codex iter-1 diff P1: online preflight MUST always overwrite provider_name from
267:         # the resolver, because _role_pins() previously pre-seeded provider_name from the
268:         # env's first entry (now changed to empty, but the always-overwrite invariant is
269:         # the defense-in-depth — any future caller passing a non-empty provider_name still
270:         # gets re-resolved at preflight, so the persisted pin reflects the actual resolution).
271:         # Offline tests skip the resolver; if provider_name is empty under offline, fall
272:         # back to the env's first entry (test-compat — tests still drive the pipeline via
273:         # OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ORDER and expect the served provider to match the pin).
274:         if not offline:
275:             rp.provider_name = resolve_role_provider(rp.model_slug, provider_order_list)
276:         elif not rp.provider_name and provider_order_list:
277:             rp.provider_name = provider_order_list[0]
278:     # I-bug-946 (Codex iter 2 P2#3 + iter-1 diff P2#2): enforce that the effective
279:     # entailment model equals the effective evaluator model. Compare EFFECTIVE values
280:     # (with their defaults) so a single env override that diverges from the default still
281:     # fails closed — not only the "both env vars set divergently" case.
282:     _DEFAULT_ENTAILMENT_MODEL = "z-ai/glm-5.1"  # I-arch-003 #1253: sovereign mirror (was stale gemma)
283:     _DEFAULT_EVALUATOR_MODEL = "z-ai/glm-5.1"   # I-arch-003 #1253: sovereign mirror (was stale gemma)
284:     eff_entail = (os.environ.get("PG_ENTAILMENT_MODEL") or _DEFAULT_ENTAILMENT_MODEL).strip()
285:     eff_eval = (os.environ.get("PG_EVALUATOR_MODEL") or _DEFAULT_EVALUATOR_MODEL).strip()
286:     if eff_entail != eff_eval:
287:         raise GateError(
288:             f"effective PG_ENTAILMENT_MODEL={eff_entail!r} != effective PG_EVALUATOR_MODEL"
289:             f"={eff_eval!r}; the gate cannot pin two different evaluator-family models"
290:         )
291:     # I-meta-001 (#933) Step 9: enforce architecture coverage at preflight.
292:     # If config/architecture/polaris_runtime_lock.yaml exists, its required_roles set
293:     # MUST match the role_pins set (every locked role pinned). Gate refuses if missing.
294:     # offline=True implies test mode (unit fixtures intentionally use 2-role pins);
295:     # tests can also explicitly opt out via enforce_architecture_coverage=False.
296:     _enforce_coverage = enforce_architecture_coverage and not offline
297:     arch_coverage = (
298:         _assert_architecture_coverage(role_pins) if _enforce_coverage
299:         else {"status": "skipped", "missing_roles": [], "lock_status": None,
300:               "warning": "architecture coverage check skipped (offline=True or enforce=False)"}
301:     )
302:     cfg = build_effective_config(control_vars, salt)
303:     return {
304:         "effective_config": cfg,
305:         "effective_config_hash": effective_config_hash(cfg),
306:         "control_vars": control_vars,             # the RESOLVED surface (post-run rebuilds from this)
307:         "control_source_map": source_map or {},   # name -> [file:line, ...] provenance (Codex P2)
308:         "role_pins": [vars(rp) | {"surrogate_fields": list(rp.surrogate_fields)} for rp in role_pins],
309:         "architecture_coverage": arch_coverage,  # I-meta-001 Step 9
310:         "reachability_checked": reachability_prober is not None,
311:         "openrouter_allow_fallbacks": False,
312:         "openrouter_provider_order": order,
313:     }

316: def _assert_architecture_coverage(role_pins: list) -> dict:
317:     """I-meta-001 (#933) Step 9: refuse the smoke unless every locked architecture role
318:     is present in role_pins.
319: 
320:     Loads ``config/architecture/polaris_runtime_lock.yaml``. If the lock exists AND
420: def resolve_role_provider(model_slug: str, provider_order: list[str]) -> str:
421:     """I-bug-946 (#932): resolve a role's served provider at preflight.
422: 
423:     OpenRouter's GET /api/v1/models/<id>/endpoints returns the providers that actually serve
424:     a model. Smoke #15 demonstrated that without per-role resolution, OpenRouter silently
425:     routes a role to a provider OUTSIDE the env-pinned order (gemma is not on Fireworks, so
426:     the evaluator was routed to Novita despite `OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ORDER=fireworks` +
427:     `allow_fallbacks=false`). The gate caught it correctly; the pin model was wrong.
428: 
429:     Algorithm:
430:       1. Fetch /api/v1/models/<id>/endpoints; parse `data.endpoints`.
431:       2. Eligible = endpoints with status absent OR status==0. status != 0 means degraded /
432:          lower-priority per OpenRouter docs (Codex iter-2 P2#4).
433:       3. Intersect eligible providers (case-insensitive) with `provider_order`.
434:       4. Return the catalog-cased provider_name of the FIRST match in `provider_order`.
435:       5. Fail closed with diagnostic if no match OR endpoints list is empty.
436: 
437:     Codex APPROVE iter 2 on choice C, brief at .codex/I-bug-946/brief_iter2.md.
438:     """
439:     import requests
440:     api_key = os.environ.get("OPENROUTER_API_KEY")
441:     headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {api_key}"} if api_key else {}
442:     url = f"https://openrouter.ai/api/v1/models/{model_slug}/endpoints"
443:     try:
444:         r = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=20)
445:         r.raise_for_status()
446:         endpoints = r.json().get("data", {}).get("endpoints", [])
447:     except Exception as exc:
448:         raise GateError(f"OpenRouter endpoints catalog unreachable for {model_slug!r}: {exc}") from exc
449:     if not endpoints:
450:         raise GateError(f"OpenRouter has no endpoints for model {model_slug!r} (model offline?)")
451:     eligible: list[str] = []
452:     for ep in endpoints:
453:         status = ep.get("status")
454:         if status is None or status == 0:
455:             name = ep.get("provider_name")
456:             if name:
457:                 eligible.append(name)
458:     if not eligible:
459:         raise GateError(
460:             f"OpenRouter has no eligible (status==0) endpoints for {model_slug!r}; "
461:             f"all endpoints degraded"
462:         )
463:     eligible_lower = {n.lower(): n for n in eligible}  # case-insensitive lookup, catalog cased value
464:     for wanted in provider_order:
465:         catalog_cased = eligible_lower.get(wanted.strip().lower())
466:         if catalog_cased is not None:
467:             return catalog_cased
468:     raise GateError(
469:         f"OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ORDER={provider_order!r} has no intersection with eligible "
470:         f"endpoints for {model_slug!r}; available: {sorted(set(eligible))}"
471:     )
472:

520:             return r.status_code == 200
521:     except Exception:
522:         return False
523:     return False

540:     """REAL generate_structured call on the default generator/searcher slug (OPENROUTER_DEFAULT_MODEL —
541:     the deepseek reasoning-first model whose structured-output 404 was the FX-01 keystone). Returns
542:     True iff a schema object parses; raises GateError on the NoEndpointError/404 class. Tiny schema +
543:     budget keep it cheap; the 404 failure path returns immediately (before any generation).
544: 
545:     ASYNC (Codex iter-1 P1): awaited directly by the async behavioral_canary() — NOT wrapped in
546:     asyncio.run(), which raises RuntimeError inside run_gate_b_query's already-running event loop and
547:     would block every healthy live run."""

622: def family_from_model(model_name: str, override: str = "") -> str:
623:     """Derive the training-lineage family from an OpenRouter model name.
624: 
625:     Returns the family label ("deepseek", "qwen", "glm", "llama", "gemma",
626:     "mistral", "kimi", "openai", "anthropic", "google-closed") or
627:     "unknown" if no prefix matches.
628: 
629:     A non-empty `override` bypasses prefix matching. Use it when a model
630:     has been renamed or when a fine-tune needs its base-family tag.
631:     """
632:     if override:
633:         return override.strip().lower()
634:     if not model_name:
635:         return "unknown"
636:     m = model_name.strip().lower()
637:     for family, prefixes in _FAMILY_PREFIXES.items():
638:         for prefix in prefixes:
639:             if m.startswith(prefix.lower()):
640:                 return family
641:     return "unknown"
642: 
643: 
644: def check_family_segregation(
645:     generator_model: str | None = None,
646:     evaluator_model: str | None = None,
647:     generator_override: str | None = None,
648:     evaluator_override: str | None = None,
649: ) -> tuple[str, str]:
650:     """Fail fast if generator and evaluator are in the same family.
651: 
652:     Returns (generator_family, evaluator_family) on success.
653:     Raises RuntimeError if same family or if either is "unknown" without
654:     an explicit override (so misconfiguration is visible at init time).
655: 
656:     Defaults pull from the module-level env-var settings.
657:     """
658:     gen_model = generator_model or PG_GENERATOR_MODEL
659:     eval_model = evaluator_model or PG_EVALUATOR_MODEL
660:     gen_override = generator_override if generator_override is not None else PG_GENERATOR_FAMILY_OVERRIDE
661:     eval_override = evaluator_override if evaluator_override is not None else PG_EVALUATOR_FAMILY_OVERRIDE
662: 
663:     gen_family = family_from_model(gen_model, gen_override)
664:     eval_family = family_from_model(eval_model, eval_override)
665: 
666:     if gen_family == "unknown" and not gen_override:
667:         raise RuntimeError(
668:             f"HONEST-REBUILD Phase 1c: generator model '{gen_model}' does not "
669:             f"match any known family prefix. Set PG_GENERATOR_FAMILY_OVERRIDE "
670:             f"to the training-lineage family (e.g. 'deepseek', 'qwen') so "
671:             f"family segregation can be checked. Family-distance from the "
672:             f"evaluator is the primary mitigation for evaluator-generator "
673:             f"self-bias (Play Favorites arXiv:2508.06709, DeepHalluBench "
674:             f"arXiv:2601.22984)."
675:         )
676:     if eval_family == "unknown" and not eval_override:
677:         raise RuntimeError(
678:             f"HONEST-REBUILD Phase 1c: evaluator model '{eval_model}' does "
679:             f"not match any known family prefix. Set PG_EVALUATOR_FAMILY_OVERRIDE."
680:         )
681:     if gen_family == eval_family:
682:         raise RuntimeError(
683:             f"HONEST-REBUILD Phase 1c: generator and evaluator are in the "
684:             f"same training-lineage family ('{gen_family}'). This defeats "
685:             f"the purpose of two-family architecture — same-family judges "
686:             f"share blind spots and RLHF biases. Pick models from different "
687:             f"families, or document the choice with explicit PG_*_FAMILY_OVERRIDE "
688:             f"values to demonstrate you know the trade-off. Recommended pair: "
689:             f"deepseek/deepseek-v4-pro (generator) + google/gemma-4-31b-it "
690:             f"(evaluator) per loopback/audit/_open_source_models_2026.md."
691:         )
692:     return (gen_family, eval_family)
693: 
694: 
695: def validate_role_families(role_map: dict[str, str], policy: str = "all_distinct",
696:                            allowed_collisions: list[tuple[str, str]] | None = None) -> dict[str, str]:
697:     """I-meta-001 (#933): N-way family segregation for the 4-role architecture.
698: 
699:     Extends the pairwise check_family_segregation to N roles per the locked
700:     architecture (Generator + Mirror + Sentinel + Judge). All four roles must
701:     be from distinct training lineages by default; allowed_collisions overrides
702:     specific pairs if the architecture lock's family_policy permits them.

704:     Args:
705:         role_map: {role_name: model_slug}, e.g. {"generator": "deepseek/...",

1754:

1795:                     provider_block["ignore"] = gen_routing["ignore"]
1796:                 provider_block["allow_fallbacks"] = False

1800:         last_error = None

1802:         for attempt in range(MAX_RETRIES + 1):
1803:             try:
1804:                 # I-meta-008 FULL-POWER: a reasoning-first GENERATOR (DeepSeek V4 Pro) needs minutes
1805:                 # per section (observed up to 412s for one success; ~24 min worst case at the slow
1806:                 # token band). Default it to the generous writer timeout when the caller passes none,
1807:                 # so a section is never killed by the cheap 90s/shared default. The $ hard cap, NOT
1808:                 # the clock, is the spend backstop. Non-reasoning-first models keep the standard default.
1809:                 _default_timeout = (
1810:                     GENERATOR_TIMEOUT_SECONDS
1950:                         "[polaris graph] Rate limited, waiting %.1fs (attempt %d/%d)",
1951:                         wait, attempt + 1, MAX_RETRIES + 1,
1952:                     )
1953:                     await asyncio.sleep(wait)
1954:                     continue
1955: 
1956:                 # I-bug-940 / I-ready-019 (#1102): a 404 has TWO causes that MUST be told apart.
1957:                 #   (a) STRUCTURAL "No endpoints found": the requested params (e.g. forced reasoning
1958:                 #       + strict json_schema with provider require_parameters) match NO provider for
1959:                 #       this slug. It reproduces on every attempt; retrying is futile. FAIL LOUD with
1960:                 #       a typed NoEndpointError so discovery callers (STORM / agentic searcher) do NOT
1961:                 #       silently swallow a dead LLM into template fallbacks (the drb_72 collapse, LAW II).
1962:                 #   (b) TRANSIENT routing miss: out-of-band probes confirmed the same call succeeds
1963:                 #       ~8s later — retry with backoff like 429.
1964:                 # A non-structural 404 that survives ALL retries is treated as structural (a config
1965:                 # error that never clears), so it also fails loud rather than re-raising a bare 404.
1966:                 if status == 404:
1967:                     _body_text = ""
1968:                     try:
1969:                         _body_text = exc.response.text or ""
1970:                     except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — body read must never mask the 404 itself
1971:                         _body_text = ""
1972:                     _structural = "no endpoints found" in _body_text.lower()
1973:                     if _structural or attempt >= MAX_RETRIES:
1974:                         self.usage.total_errors += 1
1975:                         logger.error(
1976:                             "[polaris graph] I-ready-019: STRUCTURAL 404 for model=%s "
1977:                             "(structural=%s, attempt %d/%d) — FAILING LOUD, not silent fallback. "
1978:                             "Body: %s",
1979:                             self.model, _structural, attempt + 1, MAX_RETRIES + 1, _body_text[:200],
1980:                         )
1981:                         # I-obs-001 #1141 AC3: dead-discovery 404 capture — the NAMED §-1.1 forensic
1982:                         # target (structural no-endpoint). No parsed `data`; capture status + body text.
1983:                         _io_sink = current_raw_io_sink()
1984:                         if _io_sink is not None:
1985:                             try:
1986:                                 _io_sink.record(
1987:                                     call_id=uuid.uuid4().hex, call_type=call_type,
1988:                                     role=_pathb_capture.current_llm_role(),
1989:                                     request={**body, "messages": sanitized_messages},
1990:                                     raw_response={
1991:                                         "status_code": exc.response.status_code,
1992:                                         "body_text": (_body_text or "")[:4000],
1993:                                     },
1994:                                     duration_ms=None, status="no_endpoint",
1995:                                 )
1996:                             except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001
1997:                                 pass
1998:                         raise NoEndpointError(
1999:                             f"OpenRouter 404 'No endpoints found' for model {self.model}: the "
2000:                             f"requested parameters match no provider (structural={_structural}). "
2001:                             f"Config error, not transient — fix the call shape / provider routing."
2002:                         ) from exc
2003:                     wait = RETRY_BACKOFF_BASE ** (attempt + 1)
2004:                     logger.warning(
2005:                         "[polaris graph] I-bug-940: 404 (transient provider routing), "
3050:                             f"no extractable answer. Provider misrouted output."
3051:                         )
3052: 
3053:         return result

3055:     async def generate_structured(
3056:         self,
3057:         prompt: str,
3058:         schema: Type[T],
3059:         system: str = "",
3060:         max_tokens: int = 8192,
3061:         timeout: Optional[float] = None,
3062:         reasoning_enabled: bool = False,
3063:         reasoning_effort: str = "high",
3064:         reasoning_max_tokens: Optional[int] = None,
3065:         reasoning_exclude: Optional[bool] = None,
3066:     ) -> T:
3067:         """
3068:         Structured output call — reasoning OFF by default, returns parsed schema.
3069: 
3070:         When reasoning is DISABLED and PG_STRICT_JSON_SCHEMA=1 (default),
3071:         sends response_format with json_schema + strict:true to enforce
3072:         schema compliance at the provider level (Qwen 3.5 Plus supports this).
3073: 
3074:         When reasoning is ENABLED, relies on prompt-based JSON extraction
3075:         because thinking + json_schema response_format are incompatible.
3076: 
3077:         FIX-QM1: When reasoning IS explicitly enabled, checks both content
3078:         and reasoning_content for JSON (some models put JSON in reasoning).
3079:         """
3080:         # Use strict:true JSON schema when reasoning is disabled and env allows.
3081:         # Qwen3.5-Plus supports strict schema enforcement. Gate behind
3082:         # PG_STRICT_JSON_SCHEMA (default "1") for backwards compatibility.
3083:         # When reasoning is enabled, skip — thinking + json_schema are incompatible.
3084:         #
3085:         # FIX-GLM5-STRUCTURED (2026-04-12): For models in _ALWAYS_REASON_MODELS,
3086:         # reasoning is forced ON by _call() regardless of this parameter. Without
3087:         # this check, GLM 5.1 receives BOTH response_format=json_schema strict:true
3088:         # AND reasoning=enabled, which causes complex-schema calls (StormOutlinePlan,
3089:         # SourceAnalysisBatch, ReportOutline) to dump 17K+ chars of prose into
3090:         # reasoning_content with content="" (empty). Symptom in PG_TEST_090 trace:
3091:         # "Content empty for structured:StormOutlinePlan, reasoning has 17958 chars".
3092:         # The fix makes generate_structured aware that these models always reason,
3093:         # so it skips response_format and uses prompt-based JSON extraction (which
3094:         # works because the prompt's json_hint instructs JSON-only output).
3095:         #
3096:         # I-ready-018 (#1100 keystone): the gate originally checked _ALWAYS_REASON_MODELS
3097:         # (GLM-only). But _call()'s REQUEST-side switch (line ~1474) forces a reasoning block
3098:         # for the WIDER _REASONING_FIRST_MODELS set, which also includes the reasoning-first
3099:         # deepseek default (deepseek-v4-pro / -v4-flash). For those models _effective_reasoning
3100:         # was False here, so generate_structured attached response_format=json_schema strict:true
3101:         # WHILE _call() forced reasoning -> with provider require_parameters:true + the generator
3102:         # provider pin, OpenRouter found no endpoint serving both and returned 404 "No endpoints
3103:         # found", killing STORM persona-gen and every agentic-searcher round-analysis (drb_72
3104:         # forensic: discovery 100% dead from LLM call #1, while the SAME slug served 31 successful
3105:         # generate() calls). Aligning this gate to _REASONING_FIRST_MODELS routes deepseek down the
3106:         # same prompt-based-JSON / reasoning-extraction path GLM uses (the recovery at ~2650 is
3107:         # model-agnostic), so the structured-output 404 cannot recur.
3108:         response_format = None
3109:         strict_schema_enabled = os.getenv("PG_STRICT_JSON_SCHEMA", "1") == "1"
3110:         _effective_reasoning = reasoning_enabled or (self.model in _REASONING_FIRST_MODELS)
3111:         if not _effective_reasoning and strict_schema_enabled:
3112:             try:
3113:                 json_schema = schema.model_json_schema()
3114:                 response_format = {
3115:                     "type": "json_schema",
3116:                     "json_schema": {
3117:                         "name": schema.__name__,
3118:                         "strict": True,
3119:                         "schema": json_schema,
3120:                     },
3121:                 }
3122:             except Exception as schema_exc:
3123:                 logger.warning(
3124:                     "[polaris graph] Strict JSON schema extraction failed for %s: %s "
3125:                     "— falling back to prompt-based JSON",
3126:                     schema.__name__, str(schema_exc)[:200],
3127:                 )
3128:                 response_format = None
3129: 
3130:         # Ensure system message instructs JSON output (defense-in-depth even with strict schema)
3131:         # FIX-GEMMA4: Include expected field names in JSON hint to prevent
3132:         # models from using alternative naming or nested wrappers.
3133:         try:
3134:             _schema_fields = list(schema.model_fields.keys())
3135:             _fields_hint = f" Required top-level keys: {', '.join(_schema_fields)}."
3136:         except Exception:
3137:             _fields_hint = ""
3138:         json_hint = (
3139:             "You MUST respond with valid JSON only. No prose, no markdown, "
3140:             f"no code fences — just the JSON object.{_fields_hint}"
3141:         )
3142:         messages = []
3143:         if system:
3144:             messages.append({"role": "system", "content": f"{system}\n\n{json_hint}"})
3145:         else:
3146:             messages.append({"role": "system", "content": json_hint})
3147:         messages.append({"role": "user", "content": prompt})
3148: 
3149:         result = await self._call(
3150:             messages=messages,
3151:             call_type=f"structured:{schema.__name__}",
3152:             reasoning_enabled=reasoning_enabled,
3153:             reasoning_effort=reasoning_effort,
3154:             temperature=0.5,
3155:             max_tokens=max_tokens,
3156:             response_format=response_format,
3157:             timeout=timeout or DEFAULT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,
3158:             reasoning_max_tokens=reasoning_max_tokens,
3159:             reasoning_exclude=reasoning_exclude,
3160:         )
3161:

1: """I-run11-007 (#1051): per-role OpenRouter provider routing loader.
2: 
3: Pins every verifier role (and, via the same config, the generator) to a ranked chain of HEALTHY,
4: fast providers with a deterministic fallback that NEVER routes to a broken/flaky provider — so the
5: Carney demo cannot land on the slow/empty providers that caused the runs-14/15/16 Mirror blanks.
6: 
7: The ranked order + ignore list live in `config/settings/openrouter_provider_routing.yaml`
8: (generated by `scripts/diagnostics/rank_openrouter_providers.py` from live endpoint health — LAW VI:
9: config, never inlined). This module only READS that config; it never makes a network call.
10: 
11: Degrades gracefully: if the config file or the role is absent, or routing is disabled via
12: `PG_OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ROUTING=0`, returns None and the transport keeps its prior behavior
13: (`require_parameters` only). The config is committed, so production gets pinned routing by default.
14: """
15: 
16: from __future__ import annotations
17: 
18: import os
19: from pathlib import Path
20: 
21: import yaml
22: 
23: _DEFAULT_CONFIG_PATH = "config/settings/openrouter_provider_routing.yaml"
24: _ENABLE_ENV = "PG_OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ROUTING"
25: _CONFIG_PATH_ENV = "PG_PROVIDER_ROUTING_CONFIG"
26: 
27: # Cache keyed by the RESOLVED path string so a test that repoints _CONFIG_PATH_ENV picks up its
28: # fixture rather than a stale parse. A small YAML, so a per-distinct-path parse is cheap.
29: _cache: dict[str, dict] = {}
30: 
31: 
32: def _enabled() -> bool:
33:     return os.getenv(_ENABLE_ENV, "1").strip().lower() in ("1", "true", "yes", "on")
34: 
35: 
36: def _full_config() -> dict:
37:     path = os.getenv(_CONFIG_PATH_ENV, _DEFAULT_CONFIG_PATH)
38:     if path in _cache:
39:         return _cache[path]
40:     p = Path(path)
41:     data = yaml.safe_load(p.read_text(encoding="utf-8")) if p.is_file() else {}
42:     result = data if isinstance(data, dict) else {}
43:     _cache[path] = result
44:     return result
45: 
46: 
47: def _roles_config() -> dict:
48:     roles = _full_config().get("roles")
49:     return roles if isinstance(roles, dict) else {}
50: 
51: 
52: def slug_for_provider(provider: str | None) -> str | None:
53:     """Map a served `provider` DISPLAY name (OpenRouter response field, e.g. 'AtlasCloud', 'Io Net')
54:     back to the routing SLUG ('atlas-cloud', 'io-net') that `provider.order`/`ignore` use, via the
55:     config's `provider_aliases` map. Falls back to a lower/space-fold for providers not in the map.
56:     Returns the input unchanged if falsy. (Codex diff-gate iter-1 P1: a naive fold mis-maps camelCase
57:     providers, so the empty-retry could ignore an identity OpenRouter does not match -> retry the same
58:     blank provider.)"""
59:     if not provider:
60:         return provider
61:     aliases = _full_config().get("provider_aliases")
62:     if isinstance(aliases, dict) and provider in aliases:
63:         return str(aliases[provider])
64:     return provider.strip().lower().replace(" ", "-")
65: 
66: 
67: def reset_cache() -> None:
68:     """Drop the parsed-config cache (tests that swap the config fixture call this)."""
69:     _cache.clear()
70: 
71: 
72: def role_provider_routing(role: str) -> dict | None:
73:     """Return ``{"order": [slug...], "ignore": [slug...]}`` for ``role``, else ``None``.
74: 
75:     ``None`` means "not configured / disabled" — the caller keeps its prior provider block.
76:     A configured role MUST have a non-empty ``order`` (an empty order would pin nothing); an empty
77:     or missing ``ignore`` is fine.
78:     """
79:     if not _enabled():
80:         return None
81:     cfg = _roles_config().get(role)
82:     if not isinstance(cfg, dict):
83:         return None
84:     order = [str(s) for s in (cfg.get("order") or []) if str(s).strip()]
85:     if not order:
86:         return None
87:     ignore = [str(s) for s in (cfg.get("ignore") or []) if str(s).strip()]
88:     return {"order": order, "ignore": ignore}
89: 
90: 
91: def apply_provider_routing(provider_block: dict, role: str) -> dict:
92:     """Merge the role's ranked order + ignore + ``allow_fallbacks: False`` into ``provider_block``.
93: 
94:     ``allow_fallbacks: False`` (per the OpenRouter routing docs) restricts attempts to EXACTLY the
95:     listed healthy providers in rank order — OpenRouter never falls through to an unlisted flaky
96:     provider. ``ignore`` is the belt-and-suspenders deny-list. A pre-existing ``require_parameters``
97:     is preserved. No-op (returns the block unchanged) when the role is unconfigured.
98:     """
99:     routing = role_provider_routing(role)
100:     if routing is None:
101:         return provider_block
102:     provider_block["order"] = routing["order"]
103:     if routing["ignore"]:
104:         # merge, do not clobber, any pre-set ignore
105:         existing = provider_block.get("ignore") or []
106:         provider_block["ignore"] = list(dict.fromkeys([*existing, *routing["ignore"]]))
107:     provider_block["allow_fallbacks"] = False
108:     return provider_block

2707:         reasoning-trace generator context in a ``finally``, so each
2708:         ``generate()`` invocation's call-context is scoped to exactly that
2709:         call. Without this, a later non-generator ``generate()`` in the same

2711:         stale generator context and mislabeled.

2726:             # internal COT-2 retry leg runs inside _generate_impl, so it still

66: `response.choices[0].message.reasoning` (NOT `reasoning_content` and NOT an inline `<think>`
67: block) — see https://openrouter.ai/docs/guides/best-practices/reasoning-tokens. The reused
68: `_parse_response` reads only `reasoning_content` / `<think>`, so it would LOSE the OpenRouter
69: reasoning. This transport therefore uses its OWN `_parse_openrouter_response` which adds the
70: `message.reasoning` field to the reasoning-extraction precedence
71: (`reasoning_content` -> `message.reasoning` -> leading inline `<think>`). The reasoning is
72: surfaced to `RoleResponse.reasoning` (kept SEPARATE from `raw_text`) AND stripped OUT of the
73: Path-B capture channel (`_sanitize_raw_for_capture` now also pops `reasoning`), so verifier
74: reasoning is never lost from `four_role_role_calls.jsonl` and never leaks into capture.
75: 
76: Reasoning vs output MUST stay separate (I-meta-002-q1b): `RoleResponse.reasoning` carries the
77: verifier's chain-of-thought; `RoleResponse.raw_text` carries ONLY the bare verdict/body the
78: verdict parsers consume. This is enforced by `_parse_openrouter_response` (which reuses
79: `_separate_reasoning` + the post-split blank guard).
80: 
81: No-spend / no-network-in-tests boundary: the `httpx.Client` is DEPENDENCY-INJECTED via the
82: constructor (same pattern as `OpenAICompatibleRoleTransport`). Tests pass
83: `httpx.Client(transport=httpx.MockTransport(...))` so there is NO socket in any pytest path.
84: 
85: Fail loud (LAW II): a missing `OPENROUTER_API_KEY`, a non-resolving role slug, a non-200 HTTP
86: status, or a malformed body raises (never a silent empty `RoleResponse`).

167: # `benchmark_verifier_family` derives the ACTIVE family from the ACTIVE slug (so a

169: # leaves this lane. Without that, an override like `PG_JUDGE_MODEL=z-ai/glm-5.1` would serve the
170: # Judge and Mirror as the SAME family while a static map still read "qwen" and the
171: # 4-distinct-family check passed — a clinical-lethal self-verify collision (CLAUDE.md §9.1)
172: # slipping past the gate. The family is the slug's provider prefix (`provider/model`): for all
173: # four lineup members `slug.split("/")[0]` IS the family (z-ai / ibm-granite / qwen / deepseek).
174: _BENCHMARK_VERIFIER_DEFAULT_FAMILY = {

177:     "sentinel": "minimax",

181: 
182: def _family_from_slug(slug: str) -> str:
183:     """The family lineage of an OpenRouter slug = its `provider/` prefix (fail loud if absent).
184: 
185:     Every OpenRouter slug is `provider/model`; the provider prefix IS the family lineage the
186:     4-distinct-family invariant is asserted over (z-ai / ibm-granite / qwen / deepseek). A slug
187:     with no `/` cannot have its family determined — raise rather than guess (LAW II fail-loud).
188:     """
189:     provider, sep, _ = slug.partition("/")
190:     if not sep or not provider:
191:         raise ValueError(
192:             f"benchmark verifier slug {slug!r} is not a `provider/model` OpenRouter slug; its "
193:             "family lineage cannot be determined (fail-closed — the 4-distinct-family invariant "
194:             "must assert on a real family)."
195:         )
196:     return provider
197: 
198: 
199: def benchmark_verifier_slug(role: str) -> str:
200:     """Resolve a verifier role's BENCHMARK-STAGE OpenRouter slug (P1-1, LAW VI).
201: 
202:     Sources `PG_<ROLE>_MODEL` (the lock's per-role `env_vars.primary`), DEFAULTING to the
203:     operator-chosen role_selection_final.md OpenRouter slug. This is the benchmark lineup —
204:     DISTINCT from the lock's self-host `_lock_model_slug` for Mirror + Sentinel (see module
205:     docstring). The generator/unknown role raises (it is not served by this transport).
206:     """
207:     if role == _EXCLUDED_ROLE:
208:         raise ValueError(
209:             f"role {role!r} is not served by this transport — the generator runs on OpenRouter "
210:             "via openrouter_client.py, upstream of the per-claim verifier path."
211:         )
212:     if role not in _SERVED_ROLES:
213:         raise ValueError(
214:             f"role {role!r} is not a benchmark-stage verifier role {_SERVED_ROLES}"
215:         )
216:     return os.getenv(_BENCHMARK_LINEUP_ENV[role], _BENCHMARK_LINEUP_DEFAULT_SLUG[role])
217: 
218: 
219: def benchmark_verifier_lineup() -> dict[str, str]:
220:     """Return the active `{mirror,sentinel,judge: benchmark_slug}` map (P1-1, LAW VI).
221: 
222:     The SINGLE source of truth for the benchmark-stage verifier slugs, consumed by BOTH the
223:     transport's `openrouter_role_endpoint` (the slug it POSTs as `body["model"]`) AND
224:     run_gate_b.py's `verifier_model_slugs` (the slug it pins into `RoleRequest.model_slug`), so
225:     served (the slug sent) == pinned (the slug in the request/gate) on the OpenRouter path.
226:     """
227:     return {role: benchmark_verifier_slug(role) for role in _SERVED_ROLES}
228: 
229: 
230: def benchmark_verifier_family(role: str) -> str:
231:     """Return the ACTIVE BENCHMARK-lineup family for a verifier `role` (the active-lineup family
232:     the 4-distinct-family check asserts on, NOT the lock's). The generator/unknown role raises.
233: 
234:     The family is derived from the ACTIVE slug (`benchmark_verifier_slug`, which honors the
235:     `PG_<ROLE>_MODEL` override) — NOT a static assumption. FAILS LOUD when an override's family
236:     leaves the role's expected default lane, so a cross-family re-pick (e.g.
237:     `PG_JUDGE_MODEL=z-ai/glm-5.1`, which would collide the Judge with the z-ai Mirror) is caught
238:     here rather than silently passing the 4-distinct-family gate on a stale static map
239:     (clinical-lethal self-verify, CLAUDE.md §9.1). An IN-LANE override (same provider prefix)
240:     passes.
240:     passes.
241:     """
242:     if role == _EXCLUDED_ROLE:
243:         raise ValueError(
244:             f"role {role!r} is the generator — its family is sourced from the lock, not the "
245:             "benchmark verifier lineup."
246:         )
247:     if role not in _SERVED_ROLES:
248:         raise ValueError(
249:             f"role {role!r} is not a benchmark-stage verifier role {_SERVED_ROLES}"
250:         )
251:     active_family = _family_from_slug(benchmark_verifier_slug(role))
252:     expected_family = _BENCHMARK_VERIFIER_DEFAULT_FAMILY[role]
253:     if active_family != expected_family:
254:         raise ValueError(
255:             f"benchmark verifier role {role!r}: active slug family {active_family!r} (from "
256:             f"{_BENCHMARK_LINEUP_ENV[role]}={benchmark_verifier_slug(role)!r}) leaves the "
257:             f"expected lane {expected_family!r}. A cross-family re-pick risks a self-verify "
258:             f"collision with another role (CLAUDE.md §9.1, all_distinct); fix the override or "
259:             f"update the lineup default (fail-closed)."
260:         )
261:     return active_family
262: 
263: 
264: # === STAGE annotation (P2, I-meta-007d diff-gate iter-1) =====================================
265: # A machine-readable stage marker so a future gate/manifest reader can never mistake an
266: # OpenRouter BENCHMARK run for the sovereign self-host serving path (the lock's
267: # serving_route: vast_self_host*). Surfaced in the four-role manifest stage block by the caller.
268: FOUR_ROLE_STAGE = "benchmark_openrouter"
269: 
270: # Reasoning REQUEST param for MAX reasoning (operator directive: MAX reasoning at the benchmark
271: # stage). Mirrors openrouter_client._call_impl's `reasoning_enabled` branch
272: # (openrouter_client.py:1424): `{"effort": reasoning_effort, "enabled": True}`. OpenRouter's
273: # constraint is that `effort` and `max_tokens` are mutually exclusive; "xhigh" is OpenRouter's
274: # documented MAXIMUM reasoning effort (P1-2, I-meta-007d diff-gate iter-1 — "high" is a LOWER
275: # allocation, so the prior "high" default silently DOWNGRADED the operator's MAX-reasoning
276: # directive). Source: https://openrouter.ai/docs/guides/best-practices/reasoning-tokens .
277: # LAW VI: effort is overridable via PG_FOUR_ROLE_REASONING_EFFORT (default "xhigh" = MAX).
278: _REASONING_EFFORT = os.getenv("PG_FOUR_ROLE_REASONING_EFFORT", "xhigh")
279: 
280: # I-run11-004: hard floor on the decomposition Sentinel's top-level max_tokens. The certified
281: # MiniMax-M2 call used reasoning + max_tokens>=3000; anything below that truncates the JSON
282: # {verdict, atoms} mid-emission (the run-12 truncator) and collapses every claim to a fail-closed
283: # UNGROUNDED. An env override (PG_SENTINEL_DECOMPOSITION_MAX_TOKENS) can RAISE but never lower past
284: # this floor.
285: _SENTINEL_DECOMPOSITION_MIN_MAX_TOKENS = 3000
286: 
287: # I-arch-003 (#1253) hardening (Codex gate P2): per-role CHAIN-MIN CEILING on the resolved total
288: # max_tokens (and the Mirror numeric reasoning cap). Under provider allow_fallbacks:false the binding
289: # output cap is the MIN max_completion_tokens across the role's pinned provider chain (live OpenRouter
290: # /endpoints read 2026-06-14). A budget that EXCEEDS this — whether the default or a future bad env
291: # override — would hard-400 ("requested N > max M") on the chain; that is exactly the failure class this
292: # audit closes. So every resolved budget is clamped DOWN to its chain min (env can lower for cost/testing
293: # but never raise past the provider cap). RE-DERIVE these if a role's chain in
294: # config/settings/openrouter_provider_routing.yaml is re-pinned to higher-cap-only providers.
295: _MIRROR_MAX_TOKENS_CHAIN_MIN = 131072    # glm-5.1: atlas-cloud 202752, z-ai/baidu/novita/gmicloud >= 131072
296: _SENTINEL_MAX_TOKENS_CHAIN_MIN = 131072  # minimax-m2: google/atlas-cloud 196608, novita/minimax 131072
297: _JUDGE_MAX_TOKENS_CHAIN_MIN = 262140     # qwen3.6: wandb 262144, io-net 262140
298: 
299: # I-meta-008 / #1026: blank-verdict step-down ladder. When a reasoning-first verifier returns a
300: # BLANK bare verdict (reasoning budget exhausted without converging under the high effort), retry
301: # with the effort stepped DOWN this ladder so the model is forced to spend tokens on the VERDICT,
302: # not endless reasoning. The first entry is the configured MAX effort; `None` means reasoning
303: # DISABLED (final resort — guarantees content). Overridable via PG_FOUR_ROLE_EFFORT_LADDER
304: # (comma-separated; the literal "off"/"none" -> reasoning disabled). MAX-reasoning-first, then a
305: # guaranteed verdict, then fail-loud only if even reasoning-off blanks.
306: def _parse_effort_ladder() -> tuple[object, ...]:
307:     raw = os.getenv("PG_FOUR_ROLE_EFFORT_LADDER")
308:     if not raw:
309:         return (_REASONING_EFFORT, "low", None)
310:     out: list[object] = []
311:     for token in raw.split(","):
312:         t = token.strip()
313:         if not t:
314:             continue
315:         out.append(None if t.lower() in ("off", "none", "disabled") else t)
316:     return tuple(out) if out else (_REASONING_EFFORT, "low", None)
317: 
318: 
319: _VERIFIER_EFFORT_LADDER = _parse_effort_ladder()
320: 
321: # Per-role reasoning policy (Codex iter-2 P1 — reasoning is NOT a one-size-fits-all switch).
322: #
323: # WHY per-role: Mirror (`z-ai/glm-5.1`) and Judge (`qwen/qwen3.6-35b-a3b`) are DELIBERATIVE
324: # verifiers — they weigh evidence and argue a verdict, so they get MAX reasoning effort
325: # (`xhigh`) AND `provider.require_parameters=True` (only route to a provider that honors
326: # reasoning).
327: #
328: # Sentinel is MODE-AWARE (I-run11-004): the CERTIFIED MiniMax-M2 DECOMPOSITION Sentinel
329: # (`minimax/minimax-m2`, the benchmark + lock default) was certified WITH reasoning ON and
330: # max_tokens>=3000 — turning reasoning OFF (or starving max_tokens to the 256 classifier budget)
331: # truncates the JSON {verdict, atoms} mid-emission and collapses every claim to a fail-closed
332: # UNGROUNDED (the run-12 truncator). So when the active Sentinel groundedness mode is
333: # "decomposition", the Sentinel sends MAX reasoning + a GENEROUS max_tokens, exactly replicating
334: # the certified call. The SOVEREIGN `guardian`/`noninverted` granite Sentinel modes stay
335: # reasoning-OFF (a <score>/one-word classifier whose self-host slug does not advertise
336: # `reasoning`); their settings are NOT regressed. LAW VI: overridable via `PG_SENTINEL_REASONING`.
337: # I-run11-008 (#1053): Mirror keeps reasoning ON (bake-off: reasoning-OFF DOUBLED false_bind 1->2/5,
338: # i.e. a worse grounding judge), but its reasoning is BOUNDED numerically below (effort=xhigh is a
339: # no-op on GLM, so unbounded thinking exhausted max_tokens → the 47 blanks). Overridable via PG_MIRROR_REASONING.
340: _ROLE_REASONING_DEFAULT = {"mirror": True, "sentinel": False, "judge": True}

343: def sentinel_decomposition_active(slug_override: str | None = None) -> bool:
344:     """True iff the ACTIVE Sentinel groundedness mode is "decomposition" (I-run11-004).
345: 
346:     Lazily resolves `sentinel_adapter.sentinel_groundedness_mode()` (env- + model-aware, LAW VI)
347:     so the transport can mode-gate the Sentinel's reasoning + max_tokens WITHOUT an import-time
348:     dependency on the adapter (the adapter does not import this transport — no cycle). Any
349:     resolution error is swallowed to the conservative non-decomposition answer (the certified
350:     MiniMax call is only requested when the mode UNAMBIGUOUSLY resolves to decomposition).
351: 
352:     `slug_override` (Codex diff-gate iter-4 P2) is the slug ACTUALLY being served on this call —
353:     threaded through from the request so the reasoning/max_tokens gate keys on the real served
354:     model, not a stale `PG_SENTINEL_MODEL` env, in any direct/future call path.
355:     """
356:     try:
357:         from src.polaris_graph.roles.sentinel_adapter import (
358:             _MODE_DECOMPOSITION,
359:             sentinel_groundedness_mode,
360:         )
361:     except (ImportError, AttributeError):
362:         # I-run11-010 (#1056, D4): only a genuine lazy-IMPORT failure (module missing / symbol
363:         # renamed) is safe to swallow as "not decomposition". A ValueError from
364:         # sentinel_groundedness_mode (an UNRECOGNIZED PG_SENTINEL_GROUNDEDNESS_MODE) is a caller
365:         # config bug and must NOT be silently downgraded to the 256-token classifier path (that
366:         # truncates the certified MiniMax-M2 JSON -> the run-12 all-UNGROUNDED collapse). It now
367:         # propagates (LAW II fail-loud) instead of being swallowed by a broad `except Exception`.
368:         return False
369:     return sentinel_groundedness_mode(slug_override) == _MODE_DECOMPOSITION
370: 
371: 
372: def role_reasoning_enabled(role: str, slug_override: str | None = None) -> bool:
373:     """Whether the given verifier role should send the MAX-reasoning request params.
374: 
375:     Returns the per-role default from `_ROLE_REASONING_DEFAULT`, overridable per role via the
376:     env var `PG_<ROLE>_REASONING` (LAW VI): "1"/"true"/"yes" -> True, "0"/"false"/"no" -> False;
377:     absent (or any other value) falls back to the role default. Mirror/Judge default True
378:     (deliberative verifiers -> MAX reasoning). Sentinel is MODE-AWARE (I-run11-004): in
379:     "decomposition" mode (the certified MiniMax-M2 detector) it defaults True (reasoning ON, as
380:     certified); in the sovereign granite `guardian`/`noninverted` modes it defaults False (a
380:     certified); in the sovereign granite `guardian`/`noninverted` modes it defaults False (a
381:     classifier whose slug does not advertise `reasoning`, so reasoning would break routing).
382:     """
383:     if role == "sentinel" and os.getenv(f"PG_{role.upper()}_REASONING") is None:
384:         # No explicit override: the Sentinel default is mode-aware (decomposition -> reasoning ON),
385:         # keyed on the ACTUAL served slug when supplied (Codex diff-gate iter-4 P2).
386:         default = sentinel_decomposition_active(slug_override)
387:     else:
388:         default = _ROLE_REASONING_DEFAULT.get(role, False)
389:     override = os.getenv(f"PG_{role.upper()}_REASONING")
390:     if override is None:
391:         return default
392:     token = override.strip().lower()
393:     if token in ("1", "true", "yes"):
394:         return True
395:     if token in ("0", "false", "no"):
396:         return False
397:     return default
