399: 
400: # Reuse the same timeout knob the self-host transport + openrouter_client use (LAW VI).
401: # I-meta-008 FULL-POWER: the reasoning verifiers (Mirror/Judge at effort=xhigh against a 16384-token
402: # budget) take MINUTES per claim — give them their OWN generous timeout (default 900s/15min), not the
403: # cheap 90s shared default (which also governs retrieval/embeddings). Env-overridable (LAW VI).
404: # NOTE: this is the PER-POST httpx timeout (bounds ONE network call). It does NOT bound the COMPOSED
405: # retry loop (effort-ladder x transport-retries x rate-limit-backoff), which can stack to hours per
406: # claim — that composition is bounded SEPARATELY by the #1226 wall-clock watchdog below.
407: _TIMEOUT_SECONDS = int(os.getenv("PG_VERIFIER_LLM_TIMEOUT_SECONDS", "900"))
408: 
409: # === #1226 (I-pipe-001): blank-content bound + per-call wall-clock watchdog =====================
410: # THE FAILURE: a reasoning verifier (e.g. GLM-5.1 Mirror under xhigh) can burn its whole token
411: # budget on reasoning and emit EMPTY content every attempt; combined with the per-POST 900s timeout
412: # (_TIMEOUT_SECONDS) the COMPOSED retry loop (effort-ladder/provider-failover x transport-retries x
413: # rate-limit-backoff) can stall for HOURS per claim, so the D8 4-role gate never finishes and the
414: # whole sweep hangs. Two RELIABILITY backstops (NEVER touch a verify/NLI/4-role verdict; on
415: # exhaustion they re-raise the EXISTING fail-loud BlankVerdictError/RoleTransportError -> release
416: # stays HELD; no fake/empty verdict is ever synthesized):
417: #
418: #   (1) PG_ROLE_BLANK_MAX_RETRIES (default 3): a HARD ceiling on the number of blank-content RETRIES.
419: #       Implemented by TRUNCATING the per-call effort/provider ladder to `1 + max_retries` attempts.
420: #       At the default (1 + 3 = 4) this ceiling is >= every role's existing default ladder length
421: #       (Judge 3, Mirror/routed-Sentinel 1+PG_PROVIDER_BLANK_RETRIES=4, classifier-Sentinel 1,
422: #       decomposition-Sentinel 3), so the truncation is the IDENTITY at default — it only bites when
423: #       a custom PG_PROVIDER_BLANK_RETRIES / PG_FOUR_ROLE_EFFORT_LADDER pushes a ladder past the cap.
424: #       Exhaustion fires the SAME existing `raise` at ladder-end -> the existing BlankVerdictError.
425: #
426: #   (2) PG_ROLE_CALL_TIMEOUT_S (default 3600s/1h): a COOPERATIVE wall-clock watchdog over the whole
427: #       `complete()` retry loop (checked at the top of each attempt + before each rate-limit sleep).
428: #       It does NOT interrupt an in-flight POST (httpx's _TIMEOUT_SECONDS bounds that) — it bounds the
429: #       COMPOSITION so a stuck-in-retries call aborts LOUDLY instead of hanging the sweep. 1h is a
430: #       deliberately-generous BACKSTOP against a wedged call, NOT a tight SLO: it sits well above any
431: #       HEALTHY 4-role call (a healthy claim resolves in seconds-to-minutes — the ladder rarely runs
432: #       to exhaustion, and a single blanking call returns its empty 200 quickly, it does not consume
433: #       the full per-POST 900s). The worst-case LEGITIMATE composition (every rung waiting near the
434: #       full _TIMEOUT_SECONDS, plus transport-retries and rate-limit backoff) CAN approach/exceed 1h;
435: #       that path is already pathological (it IS the stall this fix targets), so aborting it loudly is
436: #       the intended behavior, and the operator RAISES PG_ROLE_CALL_TIMEOUT_S if a slower legitimate
437: #       budget is ever needed (LAW VI). On trip it re-raises the last BlankVerdictError (if the loop
438: #       was blanking) else a RoleTransportError (both fail-loud; never a synthesized verdict).
439: #
440: # KILL-SWITCH (default-ON correct fix): PG_ROLE_BLANK_WATCHDOG (default "1"). Set "0"/"false"/"no" to
441: # REVERT to the prior behavior — when OFF neither the ladder truncation nor the watchdog check ever
442: # fires, so control flow is byte-identical to before #1226. (Reliability-only kill-switch pattern.)
443: # Read LAZILY per-call (mirrors the adjacent PG_* knobs) so an override set after import is honored.
444: _ROLE_BLANK_WATCHDOG_ENV = "PG_ROLE_BLANK_WATCHDOG"
445: _ROLE_BLANK_MAX_RETRIES_ENV = "PG_ROLE_BLANK_MAX_RETRIES"
446: _ROLE_BLANK_MAX_RETRIES_DEFAULT = "3"
447: _ROLE_CALL_TIMEOUT_S_ENV = "PG_ROLE_CALL_TIMEOUT_S"
448: _ROLE_CALL_TIMEOUT_S_DEFAULT = "3600.0"
449: 
450: 
451: def role_blank_watchdog_enabled() -> bool:
452:     """Whether the #1226 blank-bound + wall-clock watchdog is ON (kill-switch, default ON).
453: 
454:     `PG_ROLE_BLANK_WATCHDOG` "0"/"false"/"no" -> OFF (revert to pre-#1226 behavior, byte-identical
455:     control flow); absent or anything else -> ON (the default-ON correct fix). LAW VI: env-driven,
456:     read lazily so a runtime override is honored.
457:     """
458:     token = os.getenv(_ROLE_BLANK_WATCHDOG_ENV, "1").strip().lower()
459:     return token not in ("0", "false", "no", "off")
460: 
461: 
462: def role_blank_max_retries() -> int:
463:     """The #1226 hard ceiling on blank-content RETRIES (default 3 -> 1+3=4 total attempts).
464: 
465:     Clamped to >= 0 (a negative env can never produce a sub-1 attempt budget). The ladder is
466:     truncated to `1 + role_blank_max_retries()` attempts. LAW VI: env-driven, read lazily.
467:     """
468:     return max(0, int(os.getenv(_ROLE_BLANK_MAX_RETRIES_ENV, _ROLE_BLANK_MAX_RETRIES_DEFAULT)))
469: 
470: 
471: def role_call_timeout_seconds() -> float:
472:     """The #1226 wall-clock watchdog budget for the WHOLE `complete()` retry loop (default 3600s).
473: 
474:     Clamped to > 0 (a non-positive value would abort every call immediately); a non-positive or
475:     unparseable override falls back to the generous default. LAW VI: env-driven, read lazily.
476:     """
477:     raw = os.getenv(_ROLE_CALL_TIMEOUT_S_ENV, _ROLE_CALL_TIMEOUT_S_DEFAULT)
478:     try:
479:         value = float(raw)
480:     except (TypeError, ValueError):
481:         return float(_ROLE_CALL_TIMEOUT_S_DEFAULT)
482:     return value if value > 0 else float(_ROLE_CALL_TIMEOUT_S_DEFAULT)
483: 
484: 
485: def _watchdog_expired(start_monotonic: float, timeout_s: float, now_monotonic: float) -> bool:
486:     """Pure predicate: has `(now - start)` exceeded the watchdog budget? (testable in isolation).
487: 
488:     Uses a monotonic clock delta (never wall-clock, so an NTP step cannot spuriously trip it).
489:     Returns True iff the elapsed time strictly exceeds `timeout_s`.
490:     """
491:     return (now_monotonic - start_monotonic) > timeout_s
492: 
493: # I-beatboth-429 (#1173): a per-claim judge burst (~178 calls for drb_72) trips OpenRouter's
494: # rate limit on the qwen judge — a 429 (or a transient 503) on a SINGLE role call must NOT hold
495: # the 4-role release. Bounded exponential backoff-retry on the retryable HTTP statuses, honoring
496: # the `Retry-After` response header, is RESILIENCE ONLY: exhausted retries STILL raise
497: # RoleTransportError below -> release HELD (fail-closed; the gate is never weakened). LAW VI:
498: # every knob is env-driven (named, no magic numbers), read LAZILY per-call (mirrors the adjacent
499: # PG_ROLE_TRANSPORT_RETRIES pattern so an override set after import is honored).
500: _ROLE_HTTP_RETRY_MAX_DEFAULT = "5"
501: _ROLE_HTTP_RETRY_STATUS_DEFAULT = "429,503"
502: _ROLE_HTTP_BACKOFF_BASE_SECONDS_DEFAULT = "2.0"
503: _ROLE_HTTP_BACKOFF_CAP_SECONDS_DEFAULT = "60.0"
504: 
505: 
506: def _parse_retry_after_seconds(value: str | None) -> float | None:
507:     """Parse the `Retry-After` header as integer seconds (RFC 9110 delta-seconds form).
508: 
509:     Returns the non-negative float seconds on success, or `None` when the header is absent,
510:     empty, or a non-numeric/HTTP-date form — in which case the caller falls back to the capped
511:     exponential backoff. We deliberately do NOT parse the HTTP-date form (per the I-beatboth-429
512:     spec): any non-integer value is treated as the absent case so a malformed header can never
513:     yield a negative or unbounded sleep.
514:     """
515:     if value is None:
516:         return None
517:     try:
518:         seconds = int(value.strip())
519:     except (ValueError, AttributeError):
520:         return None
521:     return float(seconds) if seconds >= 0 else None

294: def preflight_openrouter_roles(http_client: httpx.Client | None = None) -> dict[str, str]:
295:     """LIVE-run preflight (openrouter mode, I-meta-007d): resolve each verifier role's BENCHMARK
296:     lineup slug against OpenRouter's catalog so a non-resolving slug fails BEFORE the sweep spends
297:     a token, AND assert the 4 families are distinct.
298: 
299:     Resolves each role's BENCHMARK slug (`benchmark_verifier_lineup` — the operator-chosen
300:     OpenRouter slugs in role_selection_final.md: Mirror `z-ai/glm-5.1`, Sentinel
301:     `ibm-granite/granite-4.1-8b`, Judge `qwen/qwen3.6-35b-a3b`; P1-1) — NOT the lock's self-host
302:     slugs (Cohere's Mirror + the granite-GUARDIAN Sentinel are not on OpenRouter). The same lineup
303:     the transport POSTs, so a slug that resolves here is the slug that gets served. Each is
304:     asserted present in the OpenRouter catalog as either an entry `id` OR its `canonical_slug`
305:     (OpenRouter exposes both; a slug may match either). Returns the `{role: benchmark_slug}` map.
306:     The `http_client` is INJECTABLE so the test feeds a faked catalog (no network). ONLY called
307:     when building the real transport (skipped when a fake transport is injected for offline tests).
308: 
309:     Fails LOUD (LAW II) on a missing slug or a family collision — never a silent skip.
310:     """
311:     assert_four_role_families_distinct()
312:     catalog = _fetch_openrouter_catalog(http_client)
313:     # Map EVERY catalog alias (entry `id` AND `canonical_slug`) -> that entry's
314:     # `supported_parameters` list. `setdefault` so the first occurrence of an alias wins (a later
315:     # duplicate id never clobbers it). A missing or non-list `supported_parameters` becomes `[]`,
316:     # which the executability check below reads as "advertises no reasoning".
317:     slug_params: dict[str, list] = {}
318:     for entry in catalog:
319:         if not isinstance(entry, dict):
320:             continue
321:         params = entry.get("supported_parameters")
322:         if not isinstance(params, list):
323:             params = []
324:         for key in ("id", "canonical_slug"):
325:             value = entry.get(key)
326:             if value:
327:                 slug_params.setdefault(value, params)
328: 
329:     resolved: dict[str, str] = {}
330:     lineup = benchmark_verifier_lineup()
331:     for role in _VERIFIER_ROLES:
332:         slug = lineup[role]
333:         if slug not in slug_params:
334:             raise RuntimeError(
335:                 f"OpenRouter catalog preflight: role {role!r} benchmark slug {slug!r} is NOT in "
336:                 f"the OpenRouter catalog (neither as an entry `id` nor `canonical_slug`). The "
337:                 "benchmark-stage OpenRouter route cannot serve it — fix the benchmark lineup "
338:                 f"(PG_{role.upper()}_MODEL / role_selection_final.md) or select "
339:                 f"{_FOUR_ROLE_TRANSPORT_ENV}={_TRANSPORT_SELF_HOST}."
340:             )
341:         # Executability check (Codex iter-2 P1): a reasoning-enabled role sends MAX reasoning with
342:         # `provider.require_parameters=True`. If its benchmark slug does NOT advertise `reasoning`
343:         # in OpenRouter `supported_parameters`, OpenRouter refuses to route (no provider honors the
344:         # param) and the FIRST call fails. Catch it here, before any token is spent.
345:         if role_reasoning_enabled(role) and "reasoning" not in slug_params[slug]:
346:             raise RuntimeError(
347:                 f"OpenRouter catalog preflight: role {role!r} is reasoning-enabled (sends MAX "
348:                 f"reasoning + provider.require_parameters=True), but its benchmark slug {slug!r} "
349:                 f"does NOT advertise `reasoning` in OpenRouter `supported_parameters` (advertised: "
350:                 f"{slug_params[slug]!r}); with require_parameters=True OpenRouter would fail routing "
351:                 f"at the first {role!r} call. Fix the benchmark lineup (PG_{role.upper()}_MODEL) to "
352:                 f"a reasoning-capable slug, disable reasoning for this role "

614: def _build_openrouter_body(request: RoleRequest, model_slug: str, normalized_messages: list[dict]) -> dict:
615:     """Assemble the OpenRouter request body: the SAME OpenAI-compatible body the self-host
616:     transport builds, MINUS the top-level `documents` key (P1-4), PLUS the MAX-reasoning param.
617: 
618:     Reuses `_build_body` for `model` + `messages` + the explicit passthrough allowlist
619:     (structured_outputs / response_format / documents / max_tokens — POLARIS-internal keys like
620:     pass2_input / citations / system never reach the body). Then (P1-4) DROPS the top-level
621:     `documents` key, which OpenRouter's chat-completions schema does not define and which would
622:     fail routing under `provider.require_parameters=True` — the evidence is already rendered into
623:     `messages` by `_normalize_messages`, so model-visibility is preserved. Then sets
624:     `reasoning = {"enabled": True, "effort": <_REASONING_EFFORT>}` — the openrouter_client
625:     `reasoning_enabled` shape (openrouter_client.py:1424). Per OpenRouter docs the mutually
626:     exclusive pair is `reasoning.effort` vs `reasoning.max_tokens`; the TOP-LEVEL `max_tokens` is
627:     NOT exclusive with effort and MUST exceed the reasoning budget. Under `effort=xhigh` the
628:     provider spends ~95% of top-level `max_tokens` on reasoning, so a popped/absent `max_tokens`
629:     starves the verdict. I-meta-008 FULL-POWER therefore SETS a generous top-level `max_tokens`
630:     (PG_VERIFIER_REASONING_MAX_TOKENS, default 16384) for the reasoning verifiers and an explicit
631:     small classifier budget (PG_SENTINEL_MAX_TOKENS, default 256) for the non-reasoning Sentinel.
632:     Source: https://openrouter.ai/docs/guides/best-practices/reasoning-tokens
633:     """
634:     body = _build_body(request, model_slug, normalized_messages)
635:     # P1-4: strip OpenRouter-unsupported top-level keys (currently `documents`). The evidence is
636:     # already model-visible in `messages` (rendered by `_normalize_messages`), so the model still
637:     # sees it; this only removes the schema-invalid body key that breaks require_parameters routing.
638:     for key in _OPENROUTER_UNSUPPORTED_TOP_LEVEL_KEYS:
639:         body.pop(key, None)
640:     # Codex iter-2 P1: reasoning is PER-ROLE. Only the deliberative verifiers (Mirror/Judge) get
641:     # MAX reasoning + `provider.require_parameters=True`. The Sentinel classifier gets NEITHER —
642:     # its OpenRouter slug does not advertise `reasoning`, so `require_parameters=True` would refuse
643:     # to route and fail the first call. See `role_reasoning_enabled` for the full rationale.
644:     if role_reasoning_enabled(request.role, request.model_slug):
645:         body["reasoning"] = {"enabled": True, "effort": _REASONING_EFFORT}
646:         # require_parameters=True makes OpenRouter ONLY route to a provider that actually HONORS the
647:         # `reasoning` param (OpenRouter's default when absent is False — it could otherwise route a
648:         # verifier to a provider that silently IGNORES reasoning, defeating the operator's
649:         # MAX-reasoning purpose). Mirrors openrouter_client._call_impl's provider block
650:         # (openrouter_client.py:1484-1487, OPENROUTER_REQUIRE_PARAMETERS default "true"). The
651:         # I-bug-946 singleton-routing half (resolved per-role provider) is M4/PENDING and
652:         # intentionally NOT here.
653:         # I-run11-007 (#1051): pin to the ranked HEALTHY provider chain (order + ignore +
654:         # allow_fallbacks:False) so a verifier call never lands on a slow/flaky provider.
655:         body["provider"] = apply_provider_routing({"require_parameters": True}, request.role)
656:         # I-meta-008 FULL-POWER (CORRECTS #1017): a reasoning verifier MUST carry a GENEROUS top-level
657:         # `max_tokens`, NOT have it popped. OpenRouter `effort=xhigh` allocates ~95% of `max_tokens`
658:         # to the reasoning budget, and `max_tokens` MUST be strictly higher than that budget so the
659:         # bare verdict has room (docs: best-practices/reasoning-tokens). It is `reasoning.effort` vs
660:         # `reasoning.max_tokens` that are mutually exclusive — NOT top-level `max_tokens`. The prior
661:         # #1017 fix popped it, so xhigh ate ~95% of an unknown provider default and STARVED the verdict
662:         # to empty for a reasoning-first Mirror (GLM-5.1) / Judge (Qwen) -> fail-loud crash on the run.
663:         # 16384 -> reasoning ~15564 + verdict room ~820 (generous for Mirror JSON + Judge enum).
664:         #
665:         # I-run11-004: the DECOMPOSITION Sentinel (MiniMax-M2, reasoning ON) emits a JSON
666:         # {verdict, unsupported_atoms, atoms} body — a multi-atom list needs MORE output room than a
667:         # bare verdict, AND the certification used reasoning + max_tokens>=3000. So the decomposition
668:         # Sentinel gets its OWN generous budget (default 16384, hard-floored at 3000 so an env
669:         # override can never re-introduce the run-12 truncation that collapses every claim to a
670:         # fail-closed UNGROUNDED). Other reasoning verifiers keep PG_VERIFIER_REASONING_MAX_TOKENS.
671:         if request.role == "sentinel":
672:             # I-arch-003 (#1253, operator "max max"): MAX output without hard-erroring. Under
673:             # allow_fallbacks:False the binding cap is the MIN max_completion_tokens across the
674:             # Sentinel provider chain (live OpenRouter read 2026-06-14): google-vertex=196608,
675:             # novita=131072, atlas-cloud=196608, minimax=131072 -> min=131072. 196608 would 400 on
676:             # the novita/minimax fallbacks, so 131072 is the safe max-of-chain (still ~8x the old
677:             # 16384 and ~40x the I-run11-004 certified 3000 floor; the multi-atom decomposition JSON
678:             # never approaches it). max_tokens is a usage-billed cap, so the generous budget never
679:             # starves output. Hard-floored at the certified minimum so an env override can't
680:             # re-introduce the run-12 truncation.
681:             decomp_budget = int(os.getenv("PG_SENTINEL_DECOMPOSITION_MAX_TOKENS", "131072"))
682:             # floor at the certified minimum, ceiling at the chain min (I-arch-003 hardening).
683:             body["max_tokens"] = min(
684:                 max(decomp_budget, _SENTINEL_DECOMPOSITION_MIN_MAX_TOKENS),
685:                 _SENTINEL_MAX_TOKENS_CHAIN_MIN,
686:             )
687:         elif request.role == "mirror":
688:             # I-run11-008 (#1053): BOUND GLM's reasoning. `effort` is a NO-OP on GLM (its OpenRouter
689:             # endpoints don't list it), so xhigh let thinking run unbounded and exhaust max_tokens ->
690:             # 47 empty-content blanks. Replace effort with a NUMERIC reasoning cap (GLM honors
691:             # reasoning.max_tokens) and give the verdict a generous total budget STRICTLY above the cap
692:             # (OpenRouter rule). Reasoning STAYS ON (bake-off: reasoning-off doubled false_bind), just
693:             # capped so it cannot starve the answer.
694:             #
695:             # I-arch-003 (#1253, operator "max max"): the 47-blank trap is specifically
696:             # reasoning_cap ~= max_tokens (reasoning eats the WHOLE budget -> empty content). The fix
697:             # is NOT a small cap per se; it is the STRUCTURAL invariant reasoning_cap << max_tokens so
698:             # the verdict always has room. Raised reasoning 4000 -> 100000 and total 24000 -> 131072
699:             # (min max_completion_tokens across the re-pinned fp8 Mirror chain: atlas-cloud=202752,
700:             # z-ai/baidu/novita=131072 -> safe-on-all = 131072). The invariant holds: 100000 reasoning
701:             # leaves 31072 for a ~50-token JSON verdict. EMPIRICALLY VALIDATED 2026-06-14 by
702:             # scripts/diagnostics/mirror_glm_provider_bakeoff.py: GLM-5.1 at reasoning_cap=100000 /
703:             # max_tokens=131072 returned 3/3 clean (0 blank, finish=stop, ~6-9s) on ALL of
704:             # atlas-cloud/z-ai/baidu/novita/gmicloud — the cap is a CEILING GLM does not exhaust, so it
705:             # never re-blanks. Do NOT collapse the gap (reasoning_cap toward max_tokens) — that re-breaks it.
706:             reasoning_cap = int(os.getenv("PG_MIRROR_REASONING_MAX_TOKENS", "100000"))
707:             # I-arch-003 hardening: keep reasoning_cap strictly below the chain-min ceiling so the total
708:             # (>= reasoning_cap + 4000) still fits the provider cap; a runaway reasoning override can no
709:             # longer push the total past the 400 boundary, and the invariant reasoning_cap << total holds.
710:             reasoning_cap = min(reasoning_cap, _MIRROR_MAX_TOKENS_CHAIN_MIN - 4000)
711:             body["reasoning"] = {"max_tokens": reasoning_cap}
712:             body["max_tokens"] = min(
713:                 max(int(os.getenv("PG_MIRROR_MAX_TOKENS", "131072")), reasoning_cap + 4000),

716:         else:

738:         # I-run11-007 (#1051): pin the non-reasoning role to its ranked HEALTHY provider chain too

1: """Semantic/NLI cross-document contradiction detector (I-ready-012 / #1079).
2: 
3: The THIRD contradiction detector, complementing the numeric-regex detector
4: (``contradiction_detector``) and the NegEx/ConText rule-cue qualitative detector
5: (``qualitative_conflict_detector``). Those two cap detection recall at the rule
6: layer: a genuine prose-only directional contradiction with NO shared number and
7: NO lexicon cue — e.g. "adjuvant chemotherapy improved overall survival" vs
8: "...provided no overall survival benefit" — passes both silently. In a clinical
9: report that is the lethal-miss class (F12).
10: 
11: This module adds an LLM-NLI pass that:
12:   1. clusters evidence rows by shared SALIENT content words computed from the raw
13:      row text (``cluster_candidate_rows``) — RECALL-oriented, independent of the
14:      rule extractors (which are blind to the no-number/no-cue rows). The cheap
15:      pre-filter bounds the O(n^2) judge cost; the judge provides precision.
16:   2. emits same-cluster row pairs (``extract_pairs``), hard-capped, highest-tier
17:      first.
18:   3. judges each pair (claim A vs claim B -> contradict/entail/neutral) and keeps
19:      ``contradict`` pairs above a confidence threshold (``detect_semantic_conflicts``).
20: 
21: Design invariants:
22:   * ADDITIVE + fail-open: a detector / judge / import / budget error logs and
23:     skips; it NEVER aborts the sweep and NEVER weakens an existing gate. It can
24:     only ADD disclosures and (via PT08) make the release gate stricter.
25:   * Default OFF (``PG_SWEEP_NLI_CONFLICT``): flag-off is byte-identical — no judge
26:     is constructed and no network call is made.
27:   * The judge is INJECTED (a ``(claim_a, claim_b) -> (label, confidence)``
28:     callable), so the detector is fully offline-testable with a fake. The
29:     production judge (``get_default_judge``) reuses the family-segregated,
30:     cost-ledgered OpenRouter substrate (``PG_ENTAILMENT_MODEL``, Gemma-4-31B by
31:     default) — the same two-family evaluator the strict_verify entailment judge
32:     uses — with a CONTRADICTION prompt. The strict_verify entailment path is NOT
33:     modified.
34: 
35: Records are shaped (``SemanticConflictRecord``) so the existing ``contradictions.json``
36: merge consumes them, and they are routed by the caller into a dedicated report
37: disclosure block + the PT08 evaluator input (the numeric renderer is untouched).
38: """

22: class SubQuery(BaseModel):
23:     """A single sub-query for search."""
24: 
25:     query: str = Field(description="The search query string")
26:     intent: str = Field(description="What this query is trying to find", default="")
27:     source_preference: str = Field(
28:         description="Preferred source type: 'web', 'academic', 'both'",
29:         default="both",
30:     )
31:     perspective: str = Field(
32:         description="STORM perspective: Scientific, Regulatory, Industry, "
33:         "Economic, Public_Health, Historical, Regional, "
34:         "Methodological, Emerging_Trends",
35:         default="General",
36:     )
37: 
38:     @model_validator(mode="before")
39:     @classmethod
40:     def normalize_subquery_fields(cls, data):
41:         """FIX-GEMMA4: Handle alternative field names from different models."""
42:         if isinstance(data, dict):
43:             for alt in ("description", "purpose", "goal", "objective"):
44:                 if alt in data and "intent" not in data:
45:                     data["intent"] = data.pop(alt)
46:             for alt in ("search_query", "text", "q"):
47:                 if alt in data and "query" not in data:
48:                     data["query"] = data.pop(alt)
49:             if data.get("intent") is None:
50:                 data["intent"] = ""
51:             if data.get("source_preference") is None:
52:                 data["source_preference"] = "both"
53:         elif isinstance(data, str):
54:             data = {"query": data, "intent": ""}
55:         return data

114:                 data["perspective_coverage"] = {str(p): 1 for p in pc if p}
115:         return data

26: _ENV_MODEL = "PG_CREDIBILITY_JUDGE_MODEL"

28: _ENV_MAX_TOKENS = "PG_CREDIBILITY_JUDGE_MAX_TOKENS"
29: # I-arch-002 (#1251): the judge model (GLM-5.1) is a REASONING model. At max_tokens=512 it burned the
30: # whole budget on its internal reasoning and got TRUNCATED mid-thought (finish=length) -> the content was
31: # a truncation-error string, not JSON -> per-row judge_error -> fail-loud (or, vs a slow provider, the SYNC
32: # call stalled in ssl.recv and FROZE the asyncio loop). Operator directive 2026-06-13: reasoning effort
33: # stays MAX, NEVER disabled. The fix is to UN-STARVE the budget so high-effort reasoning COMPLETES and then
34: # emits the JSON (measured: effort=high + 8000 tokens -> finish=stop, 4070 reasoning chars + valid JSON,

38: # Read-gap timeout (httpx). A completing high-reasoning call is ~24s; 120s leaves headroom for a slow
39: # provider while still bounding a no-bytes stall. The freeze itself is now prevented structurally by the
40: # concurrency + asyncio.to_thread offload (the call no longer runs on the event-loop thread).
41: _DEFAULT_TIMEOUT_S = 120.0
42: # Reasoning effort for the judge call (OpenRouter `reasoning.effort`). Operator 2026-06-13: MAX, never
43: # disabled — a credibility judgment with starved reasoning is "pure craps". Default HIGH (OpenRouter's top
44: # effort tier). Env may pick another VALID effort but the caller never sends an off/disabled reasoning.

115:     def call_llm(prompt: str) -> str:
116:         started = time.monotonic()
117:         json_body: dict = {
118:             "model": chosen_model,
119:             "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
120:             "temperature": temperature,
121:             "max_tokens": cap_tokens,
122:             # Operator 2026-06-13: reasoning effort stays MAX. With an un-starved max_tokens the
123:             # high-effort reasoning completes AND emits the JSON (measured: finish=stop, valid output).
124:             "reasoning": {"effort": reasoning_effort},
125:         }
126:         # PROVIDER PINNING (mirror entailment_judge): pin to the preflight-resolved evaluator provider,
127:         # allow_fallbacks=False — never silently fail over to a non-sovereign/untested provider.
128:         try:
129:             from src.polaris_graph.benchmark import pathB_capture as _pathb
130:             gate_provider = _pathb.get_role_provider("evaluator")
131:         except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — routing lookup must never break the call
132:             _pathb = None
133:             gate_provider = None
134:         # I-arch-002 (#1250): operator-directed (2026-06-13) — the open-weight judge MODEL is the
135:         # sovereign unit; the HOSTING provider may be US/China if more stable. A slow/trickling
136:         # pinned provider (allow_fallbacks=False) FROZE the whole run: this is a synchronous httpx
137:         # call on the asyncio MainThread, so a stalled SSL read blocks the entire event loop
138:         # (py-spy root cause). When PG_ROLE_ALLOW_FALLBACKS is set, SKIP the single-provider pin so
139:         # OpenRouter free-routes the model to its fastest available provider (sidesteps a slow pin
140:         # entirely — better than allow_fallbacks=True, which only fails over on ERROR, not slowness).
141:         _free_route = os.environ.get("PG_ROLE_ALLOW_FALLBACKS", "").strip().lower() in (
142:             "1", "true", "yes", "on",
143:         )
144:         if gate_provider and not _free_route:
145:             json_body["provider"] = {
146:                 "order": [gate_provider], "allow_fallbacks": False, "require_parameters": True,
147:             }
148: 
149:         # Bounded retry over the SYNC post: a transient transport fault OR an empty/truncated body is
150:         # retried (each attempt is a real billed call, cost-accounted per attempt) before the row becomes a
151:         # judge_error. httpx.Timeout bounds the read gap; the event-loop freeze is prevented STRUCTURALLY by
152:         # the caller's concurrency + asyncio.to_thread offload (this no longer runs on the loop thread).
153:         client_timeout = httpx.Timeout(call_timeout, connect=15.0)
154:         last_content = ""
155:         for _attempt in range(retries + 1):
156:             try:
157:                 with httpx.Client(timeout=client_timeout) as client:
158:                     response = client.post(
159:                         endpoint,
160:                         headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {api_key}", "Content-Type": "application/json"},
161:                         json=json_body,
162:                     )
163:                     response.raise_for_status()
164:                     data = response.json()
165:             except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — transport/parse fault: retry, else propagate to the judge
166:                 if _attempt < retries:
167:                     time.sleep(retry_backoff)
168:                     continue
169:                 raise  # judge wrapper catches -> {} -> bounded per-row judge_error (fail-loud upstream)
170: 
171:             # PATH-B two-family capture + raw-IO sink (so the gate observes this evaluator-role call).
172:             try:
173:                 if _pathb is not None and _pathb.is_active():
174:                     _pathb.capture_llm_call(
175:                         role="evaluator",
176:                         messages=[{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
177:                         raw_response=data,
178:                     )
179:             except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — capture must never break the call
180:                 pass
180:                 pass
181:             try:
182:                 io_sink = _orc.current_raw_io_sink()
183:                 if io_sink is not None:
184:                     io_sink.record(
185:                         call_id=uuid.uuid4().hex, call_type="credibility_judge", role="evaluator",
186:                         request=json_body, raw_response=data,
187:                         duration_ms=(time.monotonic() - started) * 1000.0,
188:                         # I-cred-012a iter-4 P2: label by the SERVED envelope — a malformed response (no
189:                         # choices) is the judge_error outcome (the content extract below will fail), not
190:                         # transport-"ok". Observability fidelity; does not change the abort behavior.
191:                         status=("ok" if (data.get("choices") or []) else "judge_error"),
192:                     )
193:             except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001
194:                 pass
195: 
196:             # COST + BUDGET per billed attempt (so a cap breach aborts regardless of parse) — entailment order.
197:             usage = data.get("usage", {}) or {}
198:             input_tokens = int(usage.get("prompt_tokens", 0) or 0)
199:             output_tokens = int(usage.get("completion_tokens", 0) or 0)
200:             cost = float(usage.get("cost", 0) or 0) or _orc._impute_cost_from_tokens(
201:                 chosen_model, input_tokens, output_tokens, 0,
202:             )
203:             if cost == 0 and not usage:  # degraded response, no usage block: conservative estimate
204:                 cost = _orc._impute_cost_from_tokens(
205:                     chosen_model,
206:                     _int_env(_ENV_DEGRADED_PROMPT_TOKENS, _DEFAULT_DEGRADED_PROMPT_TOKENS),
207:                     _int_env(_ENV_DEGRADED_COMPLETION_TOKENS, _DEFAULT_DEGRADED_COMPLETION_TOKENS),
208:                     0,
209:                 )
210:             _orc._add_run_cost(cost)
211:             try:
212:                 _orc.append_cost_ledger_row(
213:                     session_id=_orc.current_run_id() or "credibility_judge",
214:                     call_type="credibility_judge",
215:                     cost_usd=cost,
216:                     input_tokens=input_tokens,
217:                     output_tokens=output_tokens,
218:                 )
219:             except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — persistent ledger IO is non-critical
220:                 pass
221:             _orc.check_run_budget(0)  # raises BudgetExceededError on cap breach (MUST propagate — not masked)
222: 
223:             try:
224:                 choice0 = data["choices"][0]
225:                 last_content = choice0["message"]["content"] or ""
226:                 finish_reason = choice0.get("finish_reason")
227:             except (KeyError, IndexError, TypeError):
228:                 last_content = ""
229:                 finish_reason = None
230:             # Accept only a COMPLETE, non-empty body. Empty content OR a length-truncation (high-effort
231:             # reasoning consumed the whole budget -> the JSON never lands) is retried on a fresh call before
232:             # the row becomes a judge_error. With max_tokens=8000 a truncation is rare; the retry is bounded.
233:             if last_content.strip() and finish_reason != "length":
234:                 return last_content
235:             if _attempt < retries:
236:                 time.sleep(retry_backoff)
237:                 continue
238:         # Retries exhausted with no usable content: return it (judge wrapper -> {} -> bounded judge_error).
239:         return last_content
240: 
241:     return call_llm

3: Per-sentence check enforcing:
4:   (a) at least one provenance token present

6:   (c) span bounds are valid (0 <= start <= end <= len(text))
7:   (d) every decimal in the sentence appears in the cited spans
8:   (e) sentence and span share >= MIN_CONTENT_OVERLAP content words
9:   (f) I-bug-092: span semantically ENTAILS the sentence's specific claims
10:       (gated behind PG_STRICT_VERIFY_ENTAILMENT, defaults off)
11: 
12: Checks (a)-(e) are mechanical "provenance hygiene" — they bound a claim to
13: the same TOPIC as its span. Check (f) is "provenance correctness" — it
14: verifies the span actually entails the sentence's specific facts. The
15: audit on 2026-05-09 found that a capable generator can pass (a)-(e) by
16: producing topically-overlapping prose that introduces unsourced specifics
17: (e.g. inserting "pancreatic β-cells", "lipid metabolism", "energy storage"
18: into a span that says only "synergistic actions on insulin secretion,
19: glucagon suppression, appetite regulation, and adipocyte metabolism").

22: constructs a VerifiedSentence for use by the generator orchestrator.

102: async def annotate_nli_entailment(
103:     pairs: list[dict[str, Any]],
104: ) -> dict[str, Any]:
105:     """Score each (span ⊨ sentence) pair with the frontier LLM entailment judge; ADVISORY annotation.
106: 
107:     I-cap-003 (#1066): the scoring backend is now the project's LLM entailment judge
108:     (``src.polaris_graph.llm.entailment_judge``) — a frontier OPEN-weight model (default
109:     ``google/gemma-4-31b-it``) via OpenRouter, family-segregated from the generator, already used by
110:     strict_verify. This REPLACES the old flan-t5/minicheck path (an old/weak F1-62.1 encoder that was
111:     git-only and unavailable on the CPU VM → the previous ``nli_status:unavailable`` bug).
112: 
113:     Each pair yields a verdict ``ENTAILED | NEUTRAL | CONTRADICTED``. ``disputed`` = NEUTRAL ∪
114:     CONTRADICTED (strict_verify's contract is "no unsupported additions"; the per-sentence ``verdict``
115:     distinguishes them). Returns ``{nli_status:"ok", judge, model, sentences_checked, entailed_count,
116:     neutral_count, contradicted_count, disputed_count, disputed:[…], advisory:True}``.
117: 
118:     FAIL-LOUD only on a genuine config error: a missing ``OPENROUTER_API_KEY`` raises
119:     ``NliUnavailableError`` (surfaced as ``nli_status:"unavailable"``, never a silent pass). The judge is
120:     called SYNCHRONOUSLY (NOT offloaded to a thread) so its per-call cost accumulates in the run's
160:                 "evidence_id": pair.get("evidence_id", ""),
161:                 "reason": reason,
162:                 "sentence": pair["sentence"],
163:             })
164:             continue
165:         if verdict == "ENTAILED":
166:             entailed += 1
167:             continue
168:         if verdict == "CONTRADICTED":
169:             contradicted += 1
170:         else:
171:             verdict = "NEUTRAL"   # normalize any unexpected verdict to NEUTRAL (still disputed)
172:             neutral += 1
173:         disputed.append({
174:             "section": pair.get("section", ""),
175:             "evidence_id": pair.get("evidence_id", ""),
176:             "verdict": verdict,
177:             "reason": reason,
178:             "sentence": pair["sentence"],
179:         })
180:     scored = len(pairs) - judge_errors
181:     # If EVERY call errored, nothing was actually entailment-checked — surface nli_status:"error" LOUDLY
182:     # (not "ok" with a misleading zero-dispute count). Partial errors keep "ok" but expose the count so
183:     # an audit sees the degradation. Errored sentences are excluded from entailed/neutral/contradicted.
184:     nli_status = "error" if (pairs and scored == 0) else "ok"
185:     return {
186:         "nli_status": nli_status,
187:         "judge": "llm_entailment",
188:         "model": judge._model,
189:         "sentences_checked": len(pairs),
190:         "sentences_scored": scored,
191:         "entailed_count": entailed,
192:         "neutral_count": neutral,
193:         "contradicted_count": contradicted,
194:         "disputed_count": len(disputed),
195:         "disputed": disputed,
196:         "judge_error_count": judge_errors,
197:         "judge_errors": errors,
198:         "advisory": True,
199:     }

42: def full_control_surface(roots: list[Path]) -> list[str]:
43:     """Complete run-affecting env set = enumerated PG_*/OPENROUTER_* UNION the extra
44:     retrieval/credential env (Codex P1 — these affect the run but aren't prefix-matched)."""
45:     return sorted(set(enumerate_control_surface(roots)) | set(_EXTRA_CONTROL_ENV))

48: def control_surface_sources(roots: list[Path]) -> dict[str, list[str]]:
49:     """name -> sorted ['<relpath>:<lineno>', ...] provenance for each control var (Codex P2)."""
50:     extra = "|".join(re.escape(n) for n in _EXTRA_CONTROL_ENV)
51:     pat = re.compile(
52:         rf"os\.(?:getenv|environ\.get)\(\s*['\"]((?:PG_|OPENROUTER_)[A-Z0-9_]+|{extra})['\"]"
53:         rf"|os\.environ\[\s*['\"]((?:PG_|OPENROUTER_)[A-Z0-9_]+|{extra})['\"]"
54:     )
55:     out: dict[str, set[str]] = {}
56:     for root in roots:
57:         for py in root.rglob("*.py"):
58:             try:
59:                 lines = py.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore").splitlines()
60:             except OSError:
61:                 continue
62:             for i, line in enumerate(lines, 1):
63:                 for m in pat.finditer(line):
64:                     name = m.group(1) or m.group(2)
65:                     out.setdefault(name, set()).add(f"{py.as_posix()}:{i}")
66:     return {k: sorted(v) for k, v in out.items()}

86: def is_secret_var(name: str) -> bool:
87:     """True iff `name` is a credential whose VALUE must be redacted (not a *_TOKENS knob)."""
88:     if name in _SECRET_EXPLICIT:
89:         return True
90:     if name.endswith(("_MAX_TOKENS", "_TOKENS", "_TOKEN_BUDGET")):
130:             cfg[name] = {"secret": True, **_redact(name, val, salt)}
131:         else:
132:             cfg[name] = {"secret": False, "value": val, "set": val is not None}
133:     return cfg

136: def effective_config_hash(cfg: dict) -> str:
137:     return hashlib.sha256(json.dumps(cfg, sort_keys=True).encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()

140: def served_identity(call_metadata: dict) -> str:
141:     """Stable per-role served-identity surrogate (Codex iter-4 P1 + iter-5 P2).
142: 
143:     OpenRouter has no stable `model_version`; use provider_name + model + system_fingerprint
144:     (+ any stable router metadata), EXCLUDING volatile fields. Missing the agreed surrogate
145:     fields is caught by the caller (fatal), not silently hashed to a constant here.
146:     """
147:     stable = {
148:         k: v for k, v in call_metadata.items()
149:         if k not in _VOLATILE_METADATA_FIELDS
150:     }
151:     return hashlib.sha256(json.dumps(stable, sort_keys=True).encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()

154: @dataclass
155: class RolePin:
156:     role: str            # "generator" | "evaluator" | "mirror" | "sentinel" | "judge"
157:     model_slug: str      # FULL OpenRouter slug, e.g. "deepseek/deepseek-v4-pro" — EXACT match
158:     provider_name: str
159:     surrogate_fields: tuple[str, ...]   # the metadata fields PROVEN present at preflight
160:     canonical_slug: str | None = None   # I-bug-945 (#931): OpenRouter dated snapshot resolved
161:     # at preflight via GET /api/v1/models. The alias `model_slug` is the env-pin handle; the
162:     # canonical_slug (e.g. deepseek/deepseek-v4-pro-20260423) is what gets served as `model`
163:     # in chat completions and is the actual pre-registration anchor in pathB_gate_pin.json.
164:     # Trailing defaulted field per Codex P2#3 (don't break positional RolePin call sites).
165:     serving_route: str | None = None    # I-meta-002 PR-9/M4: the lock-sourced serving_route
166:     # for this role (e.g. "openrouter" | "vast_self_host" | "vast_self_host_bf16"). When it
167:     # starts with "vast_self_host", preflight takes the self-host branch (NO OpenRouter
168:     # resolution) and assert_post_run enforces served==pinned via _pathb_served instead of
169:     # provider_name. None / "openrouter" => the unchanged OpenRouter path. Trailing defaulted.
170:     base_url: str | None = None          # I-meta-002 PR-9/M4: the configured PG_<ROLE>_BASE_URL
171:     # captured at preflight (trailing slash stripped). assert_post_run compares the served
172:     # endpoint to THIS pinned value (drift-safe — PG_<ROLE>_BASE_URL is built via .format() so
173:     # it is not in the grepped control surface / config-drift hash). Trailing defaulted.

177:     """The served-identity surrogate over the PINNED fields only (Codex P1 — exact pin)."""
178:     picked = {f: metadata.get(f) for f in surrogate_fields}
179:     return hashlib.sha256(json.dumps(picked, sort_keys=True).encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()

373: def _role_serving_routes() -> dict[str, str]:
374:     """I-meta-002 PR-9/M4: map ``role -> serving_route`` from the runtime architecture lock.
375: 
376:     Reads ``config/architecture/polaris_runtime_lock.yaml`` (the single machine-readable source
377:     of truth). The serving_route tells preflight + assert_post_run which roles are self-hosted
378:     vLLM boxes (``serving_route: vast_self_host*``) vs OpenRouter (``serving_route: openrouter``).
379: 
380:     Degrades gracefully (Codex M4 design): a missing / unreadable lock returns ``{}`` so EVERY
381:     role falls through to the unchanged OpenRouter path. This keeps the offline
382:     generator+evaluator unit fixtures green — ``evaluator`` is not in the lock (=> not self-host)
383:     and ``generator`` is ``serving_route: openrouter`` (=> OpenRouter path unchanged). This helper
384:     is independent of the freeze in ``_assert_architecture_coverage``: it NEVER raises on lock
385:     status (the spend-freeze stays solely in that function, M4 criterion #3).
386:     """
387:     lock_path = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2] / "config" / "architecture" / "polaris_runtime_lock.yaml"
388:     if not lock_path.exists():
389:         return {}
390:     try:
391:         import yaml  # type: ignore[import-not-found]
392:         lock = yaml.safe_load(lock_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
393:     except Exception:
394:         return {}
395:     required = (lock or {}).get("required_roles") or {}
396:     routes: dict[str, str] = {}
397:     for role, spec in required.items():
398:         route = (spec or {}).get("serving_route")
399:         if route:
400:             routes[role] = str(route)
401:     return routes

405:     """True iff ``serving_route`` designates a self-hosted vLLM box (vast_self_host*)."""
406:     return bool(serving_route) and serving_route.startswith(_SELF_HOST_ROUTE_PREFIX)

409: def _self_host_endpoint_surrogate(served_model: str, served_endpoint: str) -> str:
410:     """Single-valued served-identity surrogate for a self-host role.
411: 
412:     A self-hosted vLLM response carries NO provider_name / system_fingerprint, so the served
413:     identity is the (model, endpoint) pair (Codex M4). Used for the per-role no-mid-run-drift
414:     check in assert_post_run — distinct from the OpenRouter surrogate over surrogate_fields.
415:     """
416:     picked = {"model": served_model, "endpoint": served_endpoint}
417:     return hashlib.sha256(json.dumps(picked, sort_keys=True).encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()

646: @dataclass
647: class LLMCall:
648:     call_id: str
649:     role: str
650:     prompt_messages_present: bool
651:     request_hash: str | None
652:     response_metadata: dict   # served {model, provider_name, system_fingerprint, ...}
653: 
654: 
655: def assert_post_run(
656:     pin: dict,
657:     control_vars: list[str],
658:     salt: bytes,
659:     calls: list[LLMCall],
660:     retrieval_backends_attempted: set[str],
661: ) -> dict:
662:     """Fatal post-run gate (Codex). Any violation ⇒ run INVALID, discard + re-run.
663: 
664:     Returns the established per-role served-identity surrogates on success."""
665:     # config no-drift — rebuild from the SAME resolved surface preflight pinned (not a
666:     # caller-passed list, which could differ / bypass; Codex iter-2).
667:     pinned_vars = pin.get("control_vars", control_vars)
668:     cfg_now = effective_config_hash(build_effective_config(pinned_vars, salt))
669:     if cfg_now != pin["effective_config_hash"]:
670:         raise GateError("effective_config drifted between preflight and post-run")
671:     pins_by_role = {rp["role"]: rp for rp in pin["role_pins"]}
672:     if not calls:
673:         raise GateError("no LLM calls captured — completeness check cannot pass")
674:     # COMPLETENESS: every pinned role must appear (Codex P1 — uncaptured evaluator/judge invisible)
675:     roles_seen = {c.role for c in calls}
676:     missing_roles = set(pins_by_role) - roles_seen
677:     if missing_roles:
678:         raise GateError(f"completeness: pinned role(s) with no captured LLM call: {missing_roles}")
679:     surrogate_by_role: dict[str, set[str]] = {}
680:     for c in calls:
681:         if not (c.prompt_messages_present and c.request_hash and c.response_metadata):
682:             raise GateError(f"call {c.call_id}: incomplete capture (prompt/request_hash/metadata)")
683:         rp = pins_by_role.get(c.role)
684:         if rp is None:
685:             raise GateError(f"call {c.call_id}: role {c.role!r} not pinned")
686:         # I-meta-002 PR-9/M4 self-host branch: a self-hosted vLLM verifier (Mirror / Sentinel /
687:         # Judge) carries NO provider_name — its served identity is the M1 `_pathb_served`
688:         # {endpoint, model}, which pathB_capture.build_response_metadata flattens onto the
689:         # captured metadata as top-level `model` + `endpoint` keys (provider_name/
690:         # system_fingerprint are dropped for a vLLM response). Read those flattened keys and
691:         # fail-closed assert served model == pinned model_slug AND served endpoint == the
692:         # PINNED base_url (drift-safe: PG_<ROLE>_BASE_URL is not in the config-drift hash;
693:         # comparing against the value pinned at preflight is what catches a wrong-box serve).
694:         # Missing endpoint and/or model => the `_pathb_served` block never reached capture =>

1: """Path-B gate lifecycle helper for the honest_sweep runner (I-safety-002b #925).
2: 
3: Wraps each benchmark question with the gate: preflight + register capture sink + run +
4: assert_post_run before any scoring. Persists the pin record to the run dir. Self-contained
5: so the runner diff is minimal (1 import + 1 ``with`` per question).
6: 
7: Gate-off by default: the helper is a no-op context manager when ``--pathB-gate`` is not set,
8: so the existing honest_sweep pipeline is untouched outside the benchmark.
9: 
10: Per the Codex-APPROVED brief v2 (call_impl_capture + entailment_judge_capture +
11: served_metadata_provenance) and the Codex-APPROVED PR-2 role-tag fork (Option B: capture
12: only explicitly-tagged report-generator + report-evaluator calls; auxiliary scope/inductor
13: LLMs are not gated).
14: """
15: 
16: from __future__ import annotations
17:

19: import json
20: import logging
21: import os

26: from src.polaris_graph.llm.openrouter_client import validate_role_families
27: from scripts.architecture.verify_lock import load_lock
28: from scripts.dr_benchmark.pathB_run_gate import (
29:     GateError,
30:     LLMCall,
31:     RolePin,
32:     assert_post_run,
33:     preflight,
34: )
35: 
36: logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
37: 
38: # The four locked architecture roles (config/architecture/polaris_runtime_lock.yaml).
39: # Order is generator -> mirror -> sentinel -> judge (the canonical pipeline order).
40: _LOCKED_ROLES = ("generator", "mirror", "sentinel", "judge")
41: 
42: # Per-role env-var OVERRIDE knobs, applied ON TOP of the lock-sourced default slug. Mirrors
43: # config/architecture/polaris_runtime_lock.yaml:env_vars. The generator additionally honors
44: # the legacy OPENROUTER_DEFAULT_MODEL fallback (documented honest_sweep override chain).
45: _ROLE_ENV_OVERRIDE = {
46:     "generator": "PG_GENERATOR_MODEL",
47:     "mirror": "PG_MIRROR_MODEL",
48:     "sentinel": "PG_SENTINEL_MODEL",
49:     "judge": "PG_JUDGE_MODEL",
50: }
51: 
52: 
53: def _lock_default_slug(role: str) -> str:
54:     """The role's default model_slug, SOURCED FROM the architecture lock so pins + lock cannot
55:     drift (Codex P2, accepted). Reads lock['required_roles'][role]['model_slug']."""
56:     lock = load_lock()
57:     return str(lock["required_roles"][role]["model_slug"]).strip()
58: 
59: 
60: def _resolve_role_slug(role: str) -> str:
61:     """Resolve a role's effective slug: lock default, with the per-role PG_*_MODEL env override
62:     applied on top. The generator preserves its documented PG_GENERATOR_MODEL >
63:     OPENROUTER_DEFAULT_MODEL > lock-default precedence (regression: a sweep that exports only
64:     OPENROUTER_DEFAULT_MODEL must still pin the right generator)."""
65:     default = _lock_default_slug(role)
66:     if role == "generator":
67:         return (
68:             os.getenv("PG_GENERATOR_MODEL")
69:             or os.getenv("OPENROUTER_DEFAULT_MODEL")
70:             or default
71:         ).strip()
72:     env_name = _ROLE_ENV_OVERRIDE[role]
73:     return (os.getenv(env_name) or default).strip()
74: 
75: 
76: def _role_pins() -> list[RolePin]:
77:     """Build the FOUR per-role pins (generator/mirror/sentinel/judge) from the lock + env.
78: 
79:     I-meta-002 sub-PR-5: the 2-role (generator+evaluator) pin set is replaced by the locked
80:     4-role set. The post-run gate enforces completeness in BOTH directions — every pinned role
81:     must be observed AND every observed call must be pinned (pathB_run_gate.assert_post_run
82:     lines 471/479) — so the pin set must EXACTLY match the captured roles. The 4-role pipeline
83:     emits generator/mirror/sentinel/judge calls; a leftover legacy 'evaluator' pin would
84:     therefore gate-FAIL at runtime (no evaluator call is captured). No production caller pins
85:     'evaluator' directly (only this function feeds preflight via gate_around_question), so the
86:     role is dropped here cleanly.
87: 
88:     Default slugs are LOCK-SOURCED via load_lock() (Codex P2, accepted) so the pins and the
89:     architecture lock cannot drift; per-role PG_*_MODEL env vars override on top. The generator
90:     keeps its PG_GENERATOR_MODEL > OPENROUTER_DEFAULT_MODEL > lock-default precedence.
91: 
92:     validate_role_families() runs on the effective 4-role map so the N-way family invariant
93:     (all 4 lineages distinct) holds at pin-build time — a same-family misconfiguration fails
94:     LOUD here rather than silently at runtime.
95: 
96:     Codex PR-2 diff iter-1 P1 #2: surrogate_fields are ONLY those PROVEN present in the served
97:     response (provider_name + model). assert_post_run treats a missing surrogate field as
98:     fatal; system_fingerprint is recorded when present but is NOT a required surrogate.
99: 
100:     I-bug-946 (#932): provider_name is left empty here; preflight() resolves the ACTUAL served
101:     provider per role via /api/v1/models/<id>/endpoints (the env is a candidate list)."""
102:     slug_by_role = {role: _resolve_role_slug(role) for role in _LOCKED_ROLES}
103:     # N-way family segregation on the effective 4-role map (raises RuntimeError on collision).
104:     validate_role_families(slug_by_role)
105:     surrogate_fields = ("provider_name", "model")
106:     return [
107:         RolePin(role, slug_by_role[role], "", surrogate_fields)
108:         for role in _LOCKED_ROLES
109:     ]
110: 
111: 
112: def role_tag(role: str):
113:     """Path-B capture role-tag context manager for a role-pipeline LLM call.
114: 
115:     Thin re-export of pathB_capture.llm_role so the 4-role call sites (Mirror/Sentinel/Judge)
116:     can scope their served-identity capture with the correct role string WITHOUT each importing
117:     pathB_capture directly. pathB_capture already accepts arbitrary role strings via its _ROLE
118:     contextvar, so "mirror" / "sentinel" / "judge" are supported with no capture-side change.
119:     Use as `with role_tag("sentinel"): ...`. The deep sweep call-site wiring is sub-PR-6."""
120:     return _capture.llm_role(role)
121: 
122: 
123: def _salt() -> bytes:
124:     return (os.getenv("PG_PATHB_GATE_SALT") or "pathB-default-unsalted").encode("utf-8")
125: 
126: 
127: @contextlib.contextmanager
128: def gate_around_question(
129:     *, enabled: bool, run_dir: Path, control_vars: list[str] | None = None,
130: ) -> Iterator[None]:
131:     """Wrap one benchmark question's run with preflight + post-run assertion.
132: 
133:     Usage in the runner:
134:         with gate_around_question(enabled=args.pathB_gate, run_dir=run_dir):
135:             ... process_query body, including the role-tagged LLM calls ...
136:             # On normal exit, assert_post_run runs (raises GateError if not full-power).
137: 
138:     Behavior:
139:     - enabled=False: no-op (yields immediately, no capture, no preflight).
140:     - enabled=True: preflight (raises GateError if not full-power); register_pathB_capture;
141:       yield; on normal exit, assert_post_run; persist pin + result to ``run_dir``. On
142:       exception inside the body, capture is cleared but the exception propagates.
143:     """
144:     if not enabled:
145:         yield
146:         return
147: 
148:     pin_path = run_dir / "pathB_gate_pin.json"
149:     result_path = run_dir / "pathB_gate_result.json"
150:     invalid_sentinel = run_dir / "pathB_gate_INVALID"
151:     run_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
152: 
153:     # Codex PR-2 diff iter-1 P3: write a FAIL result file even when preflight raises,
154:     # so a missing-credential / unreachable-backend failure has an explicit per-run record
155:     # (otherwise the only artifact is a stderr exception, no traceable artifact).
156:     try:
157:         pin = preflight(
158:             control_vars=list(control_vars or []),
159:             role_pins=_role_pins(),
160:             salt=_salt(),
161:             roots=[Path("src/polaris_graph"), Path("scripts")],
162:             offline=False,  # real run = real reachability ping (gate enforce-by-default).
163:         )
164:     except GateError as exc:
165:         result_path.write_text(
166:             json.dumps(
167:                 {"verdict": "FAIL", "stage": "preflight", "reason": str(exc)},
168:                 indent=2, sort_keys=True,
169:             ),
170:             encoding="utf-8",
171:         )
172:         invalid_sentinel.write_text(
173:             f"preflight FAIL: {exc}\n", encoding="utf-8",
174:         )
175:         logger.error("[pathB] preflight FAIL: %s", exc)
176:         raise
177:     pin_path.write_text(json.dumps(pin, indent=2, sort_keys=True, default=str),
178:                         encoding="utf-8")
179:     _capture.register_pathB_capture()
180:     # I-bug-946 (#932): publish the resolved per-role provider mapping via ContextVar so
181:     # openrouter_client and entailment_judge force singleton routing in their request bodies.
182:     # Without this, OpenRouter's silent fallback re-routes mid-run and the post_run gate fails
183:     # (smoke #15: evaluator served by Novita while pin expected Fireworks).
184:     role_provider_map = {
185:         rp["role"]: rp["provider_name"]
186:         for rp in pin.get("role_pins", [])
187:         if rp.get("provider_name")
188:     }
189:     rp_token = _capture.set_role_providers(role_provider_map) if role_provider_map else None
190:     try:
191:         yield
192:     except Exception:
193:         # Propagate; do not run assert_post_run on a failed run (it would mask the cause).
194:         if rp_token is not None:
195:             _capture.reset_role_providers(rp_token)
196:         _capture.clear_pathB_capture()
197:         raise
198: 
199:     try:
200:         # #958 (S2): a truncated corpus (post-fetch loop budget broke mid-corpus)
201:         # is a fail-loud non-clean signal — block PASS BEFORE the assert/PASS write.
202:         # Reuses the existing GateError handler below (→ FAIL result + INVALID sentinel).
203:         try:
204:             _manifest = json.loads(
205:                 (run_dir / "manifest.json").read_text(encoding="utf-8")
206:             )
207:         except Exception:
208:             _manifest = {}
209:         if _capture.corpus_truncated_from_manifest(_manifest):
210:             _rt = _manifest.get("retrieval", {})
211:             raise GateError(
212:                 "corpus truncated — post-fetch loop budget broke mid-corpus "
213:                 f"({_rt.get('candidates_processed')}/{_rt.get('candidates_total')} "
214:                 "candidates processed); run is partial, not full-power"
215:             )
216:         calls = [LLMCall(**c) for c in _capture.collected_calls()]
217:         backends = _capture.attempted_backends()
218:         result = assert_post_run(
219:             pin=pin,
220:             control_vars=list(control_vars or []),
221:             salt=_salt(),
222:             calls=calls,
223:             retrieval_backends_attempted=backends,
224:         )
225:         result_path.write_text(
226:             json.dumps({"verdict": "PASS", **result}, indent=2, sort_keys=True, default=str),
227:             encoding="utf-8",
228:         )
229:         logger.info("[pathB] gate PASS for run_dir=%s", run_dir)
230:     except GateError as exc:
231:         result_path.write_text(
232:             json.dumps(
233:                 {"verdict": "FAIL", "stage": "post_run_assert", "reason": str(exc)},
234:                 indent=2, sort_keys=True,
235:             ),
236:             encoding="utf-8",
237:         )
238:         # Codex PR-2 diff iter-1 P2 #2: write an INVALID sentinel so downstream scoring
239:         # (PR-3 claim_audit_scorer) can skip the run_dir's per-run artifacts even though
240:         # they were written during the run (manifest/judge/etc.). The gate is the source
241:         # of truth for run validity; the sentinel makes that machine-readable.
242:         invalid_sentinel.write_text(
243:             f"post-run gate FAIL: {exc}\n", encoding="utf-8",
244:         )
245:         logger.error("[pathB] gate FAIL for run_dir=%s: %s", run_dir, exc)
246:         raise
247:     finally:

1367: # The 5 LOCKED golden DRB-EN benchmark slugs (the issue's scope boundary). These are

1369: # resolved by filtering the EXISTING `SWEEP_QUERIES` registration (single source of

1372: LOCKED_BENCHMARK_SLUGS: tuple[str, ...] = (
1373:     "drb_72_ai_labor",
1374:     "drb_75_metal_ions_cvd",

1384: 
1385: def load_locked_questions(slugs: tuple[str, ...] | None = None) -> list[dict]:
1386:     """Resolve the locked benchmark question(s) by FILTERING the existing `SWEEP_QUERIES`.
1387: 
1388:     `SWEEP_QUERIES` (in `scripts.run_honest_sweep_r3`) is the single runtime source of
1389:     truth the sweep AND the routing tests already key off; this loader is a thin filter
1390:     over it, NOT a new question source (§0 of the I-meta-007e brief). Imported LAZILY so
1391:     importing `run_gate_b` opens no socket and pulls no big sweep file at module load.
1392: 
1393:     `slugs=None` resolves all 5 locked slugs (in `LOCKED_BENCHMARK_SLUGS` order); a tuple
1394:     resolves that subset. Each requested slug must be one of the 5 locked slugs AND present
1395:     in `SWEEP_QUERIES` exactly once with a `domain` — otherwise this fails LOUD (LAW II),
1396:     never a silent skip / empty run.
1397: 
1398:     CALLER CONTRACT (env-preservation): importing `scripts.run_honest_sweep_r3` triggers
1399:     `load_dotenv(override=False)` at its module top, which mutates `os.environ` from `.env`.
1400:     The `--list` path (enumeration-only, NO spend) wraps the CALL to this loader in an
1401:     os.environ snapshot/restore so it leaves the process env byte-identical; the real-run
1402:     path (`--only`/`--all`) lets `.env` stand because the live run needs the keys.
1403:     """
1404:     requested = LOCKED_BENCHMARK_SLUGS if slugs is None else tuple(slugs)
1405:     unknown = [s for s in requested if s not in LOCKED_BENCHMARK_SLUGS]
1406:     if unknown:
1407:         raise ValueError(
1408:             f"load_locked_questions: slug(s) {unknown!r} are not locked benchmark slugs. "
1409:             f"Valid locked slugs: {list(LOCKED_BENCHMARK_SLUGS)}."
1410:         )
1411: 
1412:     from scripts.run_honest_sweep_r3 import SWEEP_QUERIES
1413: 
1414:     resolved: list[dict] = []
1415:     for slug in requested:
1416:         matches = [q for q in SWEEP_QUERIES if q.get("slug") == slug]
1417:         if not matches:
1418:             raise ValueError(
1419:                 f"load_locked_questions: locked slug {slug!r} is NOT registered in "
1420:                 f"SWEEP_QUERIES — the loader filters the existing registration (no hardcoded "
1421:                 f"slug->question fallback). Fix the SWEEP_QUERIES registration."
1422:             )
1423:         if len(matches) > 1:
1424:             raise ValueError(
1425:                 f"load_locked_questions: locked slug {slug!r} is registered {len(matches)} "
1426:                 f"times in SWEEP_QUERIES; a benchmark slug must route to exactly one domain "
1427:                 f"(fail-closed)."
1428:             )
1429:         entry = matches[0]
1430:         if not entry.get("domain"):
1431:             raise ValueError(
1432:                 f"load_locked_questions: SWEEP_QUERIES entry for slug {slug!r} has no domain; "
1433:                 f"the 4-role builder keys the frozen contract by (domain template, slug) — a "
1434:                 f"domain-less registration cannot route (fail-closed)."
1435:             )
1435:             )
1436:         resolved.append(entry)
1437:     return resolved
1438: 
1439: 
1440: def _format_list_preview(questions: list[dict]) -> str:
1441:     """Build the `--list` / `--dry-run` preview text — NO spend, NO network, NO env mutation.
1442: 
1443:     Uses ONLY the PURE readers (`four_role_transport_mode`, `verifier_model_slugs`,
1444:     `assert_four_role_families_distinct`) — none opens a socket or mutates process env; each
1445:     reads only the in-memory architecture lock / process env. It calls NONE of
1446:     `run_gate_b_query` / `enable_four_role_mode` / `preflight_four_role_transport` /
1447:     `build_gate_b_transport`. Surfaces, for the blind operator, exactly what a real run WOULD
1448:     do before any money is authorized: the resolved questions, the active transport mode, the
1449:     4 role slugs+families, and a DESCRIPTIVE preflight plan (not an executed preflight).
1450:     """
1451:     mode = four_role_transport_mode()
1452:     families = assert_four_role_families_distinct()  # in-memory lock read; asserts 4 distinct
1453:     verifier_slugs = verifier_model_slugs()
1454:     generator_family = families.get("generator", "<unknown>")
1455: 
1456:     lines: list[str] = []
1457:     lines.append("=" * 72)
1458:     lines.append("GATE-B 4-ROLE BENCHMARK -- NO-SPEND PREVIEW (--list / --dry-run)")
1459:     lines.append("NOTHING below spends money, opens a socket, or mutates the environment.")
1460:     lines.append("=" * 72)
1461:     lines.append(f"resolved questions: {len(questions)}")
1462:     for q in questions:
1463:         domain = q["domain"]
1464:         slug = q["slug"]
1465:         prompt = (q.get("question") or "").strip().replace("\n", " ")
1466:         prompt_preview = prompt[:100] + ("..." if len(prompt) > 100 else "")
1467:         has_amplified = bool(q.get("amplified"))
1468:         amplified_note = (
1469:             f"curated amplified set ({len(q['amplified'])} entries)"
1470:             if has_amplified
1471:             else "NO curated amplified set (no-amplified stub -- elevated abort_corpus_inadequate risk)"
1472:         )
1473:         lines.append("")
1474:         lines.append(f"  - slug={slug}")
1475:         lines.append(f"    domain={domain}")
1476:         lines.append(f"    scope_template=config/scope_templates/{domain}.yaml")
1477:         lines.append(f"    retrieval={amplified_note}")
1478:         lines.append(f"    prompt={prompt_preview!r}")
1479:     lines.append("")
1480:     lines.append("-" * 72)
1481:     lines.append(f"PG_FOUR_ROLE_TRANSPORT mode: {mode}")
1482:     lines.append(f"  generator: family={generator_family} (runs upstream on OpenRouter; from lock)")
1483:     for role in _VERIFIER_ROLES:
1484:         lines.append(
1485:             f"  {role}: slug={verifier_slugs[role]} family={families[role]}"
1486:         )
1487:     lines.append("")
1488:     if mode == _TRANSPORT_OPENROUTER:
1489:         plan = (
1490:             "openrouter mode -> a REAL run would resolve the Mirror/Sentinel/Judge benchmark "
1491:             "slugs against the OpenRouter /models catalog (incl. a reasoning-capability check) "
1492:             "and assert the 4 families distinct, BEFORE spending any token."
1493:         )
1494:     else:
1495:         plan = (
1496:             "self_host mode -> a REAL run would resolve each PG_<ROLE>_BASE_URL self-hosted "
1497:             "endpoint and assert the 4 families distinct, BEFORE the sweep starts."
1498:         )
1499:     lines.append(f"preflight plan (descriptive, NOT executed): {plan}")
1500:     lines.append("-" * 72)
1501:     return "\n".join(lines)
1502:

1504: def _resolve_benchmark_upload(
1505:     upload_file: str, classification: str
1588:     `run_one_query`). Returns 0 on success, 2 on a usage/loader error, 1 if any question run
1589:     does not reach a `success`/`partial_*` status.
1590:     """
1591:     import argparse
1592: 
1593:     parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(
1594:         prog="run_gate_b",

1: """Path-B benchmark run capture (I-safety-002b #925).
2: 
3: Run-scoped capture of every LLM provider completion (all roles) + retrieval-backend
4: attempts, for the DR head-to-head gate. This module stores PLAIN DICTS; the runner
5: converts them to ``scripts.dr_benchmark.pathB_run_gate.LLMCall`` when calling
6: ``assert_post_run`` — so this module has ZERO dependency on the gate / scripts package
7: and the production hot path never imports ``scripts`` from ``src``.
8: 
9: Best-effort + gate-flagged: nothing is captured unless ``register_pathB_capture()`` has
10: been called for the current run, so when the benchmark gate is OFF the hot path pays only
11: one contextvar read. Capture NEVER raises (it must not break generation), mirroring the
12: I-gen-004 reasoning-sink pattern.
13: 
14: Served-identity provenance: ``build_response_metadata`` reads ONLY genuinely-served fields
15: from the provider response (OpenRouter ``provider`` / served ``model`` / ``system_fingerprint``)
16: and DROPS missing fields. Request-derived values are never substituted, so a response that
17: fails to report its served provider/model makes the gate fail loud (in ``assert_post_run``)
18: rather than silently pass on request-derived data.

188: # ── I-meta-002-q1d (#945): per-call retrieval trace (best-effort, no-op when not started) ──────────
189: def start_retrieval_trace(path: "Path | str | None" = None) -> None:
190:     """Begin a FRESH retrieval trace for the current query (P2 lifecycle hygiene, Codex brief-gate):
191:     a new list so a prior query's records can never leak into a later run_dir flush. Call once at the

200: 
201: def _live_append(rec: dict) -> None:
202:     """I-obs-001 #1141 AC2: best-effort APPEND of one record to the live retrieval_trace.jsonl.
203: 
204:     No-op when no path was supplied to start_retrieval_trace (every unit test / non-benchmark caller).
205:     NEVER raises (module contract: capture never raises). Append mode keeps the file a valid JSONL
206:     prefix even on a mid-run kill; the end-of-retrieval ``"w"`` flush stays the reconciling final
207:     writer, so final content/order is byte-identical on every normal exit."""
208:     path = _RETRIEVAL_TRACE_PATH.get()
209:     if path is None:
210:         return
211:     try:
212:         with _RETRIEVAL_TRACE_LOCK:
213:             with open(path, "a", encoding="utf-8") as fh:
214:                 fh.write(json.dumps(rec, ensure_ascii=False) + "\n")
215:     except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — capture NEVER raises (module contract, lines 11-12)
216:         logger.warning("retrieval_trace live-append failed", exc_info=True)

70: 
71: # Minimal English stopword list. Strict-verify's content-word overlap should
72: # count substantive vocabulary, not function words. This is intentionally
73: # small — the rule is conservative ("at least 2 shared content words")
74: # so even a short stoplist yields the right behavior.
75: _STOPWORDS: frozenset[str] = frozenset({
76:     "a", "an", "the", "and", "or", "but", "if", "of", "in", "on", "at",
77:     "to", "for", "with", "as", "by", "from", "into", "through", "during",
78:     "before", "after", "above", "below", "between", "is", "are", "was",
79:     "were", "be", "been", "being", "have", "has", "had", "having", "do",
80:     "does", "did", "doing", "will", "would", "should", "could", "may",
81:     "might", "must", "can", "this", "that", "these", "those", "it",
82:     "its", "their", "there", "they", "them", "we", "us", "our", "you",
83:     "your", "i", "me", "my", "he", "she", "his", "her",
84: })
85: 
86: _DECIMAL_RE = re.compile(r"\d+(?:\.\d+)?")
87: _WORD_RE = re.compile(r"[A-Za-z][A-Za-z0-9_\-]+")
88: 
89: 
90: def _min_overlap_threshold() -> int:
91:     raw = os.environ.get("PG_PROVENANCE_MIN_CONTENT_OVERLAP", "")
92:     try:
93:         return max(0, int(raw))
94:     except ValueError:
95:         return DEFAULT_MIN_CONTENT_OVERLAP
96: 
97: 
98: def _content_words(text: str) -> set[str]:
99:     """Lowercase content words (>=3 chars, not stopwords) from `text`."""
100:     return {
101:         m.group(0).lower()
102:         for m in _WORD_RE.finditer(text)
103:         if len(m.group(0)) >= 3 and m.group(0).lower() not in _STOPWORDS
104:     }
105: 
180:     string. Empty / unset env returns the default mode silently —
181:     that is the intended default, not a misconfiguration.
182: 
183:     I-bug-095: default mode is 'enforce' (was 'off' before this Issue).
184:     Operators who need the pre-graduation behavior can set
185:     PG_STRICT_VERIFY_ENTAILMENT=off explicitly.
186:     """
187:     raw = os.environ.get("PG_STRICT_VERIFY_ENTAILMENT", _DEFAULT_MODE).lower().strip()
188:     if raw and raw not in ("off", "warn", "enforce"):
189:         if raw not in _UNKNOWN_MODE_WARNED:
190:             _UNKNOWN_MODE_WARNED.add(raw)
191:             logger.warning(
192:                 "PG_STRICT_VERIFY_ENTAILMENT=%r unrecognized; "
193:                 "treating as %r (default). Valid: off, warn, enforce.",
194:                 raw, _DEFAULT_MODE,
195:             )
196:         return _DEFAULT_MODE
197:     return raw or _DEFAULT_MODE
198:
